**शुक्रे क्रोवानरः सौम्ये त्वन्यैः श्वाकृतयो मृगाः॥२३८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Mars is in Leo, the thought in the enquirer's mind is a tiger; and if the Sun and the Moon are posited in Leo, the idea is a lion; and if Venus in Leo, it is a dog; if Mercury in Leo, it is a monkey; and if other planets are in Leo, the prediction of an animal akin to dog can be made. 138

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**तुलागते भृगौ वत्सश्चन्द्रे गावः प्रकीर्तिताः। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**धनुःस्थितेषु जीवेन्दुकुजेषु तुरगो भवेत्॥२३९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सपुत्रेऽर्के स्थिते कुम्भे मत्तो गज उदाहृतः। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सर्पे च तत्र महिषो वानरो बुधजीवयोः॥ २४०॥**  


</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Venus is in Libra, the idea in the mind is about the loss of a calf; if it is the Moon, the idea is a cow, if Jupiter,the Moon and Mars are in Sagittarius, the idea is a horse; if along with Saturn the Sun is also in Aquarius; the thought is about a mad elephant, if Rahu is in Aquarius, it is a buffalo; and if Mercury and Jupiter are in Aquarius it is a monkey. 139–140

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**शुक्रामृतांशुसूर्येषु स्थितेषु पशुरुच्यते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जीवसूर्येक्षिते गर्भो वन्ध्या रविजवीक्षिते। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अङ्गारकेक्षिते शुष्कमिति ज्ञात्वा वदेत्सुधीः॥१४१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If in Aquarius are posited Venus, the Sun and the Moon, the idea is a cow; if Jupiter and the Sun aspect Aquarius, it is a pregnant cow; if aspected by Saturn, it is a barren cow; and if aspected by Mars, it is an old cow with no more calving. Such predictions can possibly be made by a wise man. 141

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**वक्ष्येहं चिन्तनां सूक्ष्मां जनैस्तु परिचिन्तिताम्। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**धिषणे कुम्भराशिस्ये त्रिकोणेवाथ पश्यति। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्मृतो गजस्तथा मीनधनुषी वीक्षिते शुभैः॥ २४२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If a person has something in his mind and he asks the astrologist to predict it, the method of detecting it is called ‘chintanaa’, which is detailed below:

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 This is a subtle subject which is going to be described. If Jupiter is in Aquarius or in its trines, *i.e*. in Gemini andLibra, or if Jupiter aspects these signs, the person has an elephant in his mind; and the same answer can be given if benefic planets aspect Pisces and Sagittarius. 142

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्मृतः कपिर्मेषगते शनौ ब्रूयान्मतङ्गजम्। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कुजे मेषगते छागः बुधे नर्तकगायकौ॥२४३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Saturn is in Aries, the idea thought about is a monkey or an elephant. If it is Mars in Aries, the thought is a goat. If Mercury, is in Aries, it is a dancer or a singer 143

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**गुरुशुक्रदिनेशेषु वणिजं वस्त्रजीविनम्।  
चन्द्रे तथा वदेन्मन्दे सिह्मस्थे रिपुचिन्तनम्॥ १४४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Jupiter, Venus and the Sun are in Aries, the idea is a textile merchant; and the same is the answer if the Moon is in Aries; if Saturn is in Leo, the person is thinking of his enemy. 144

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**वृषस्थे महिषो तौलौ चक्रिणं वृश्चिके गदम्। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मेषगे सूर्यतनये मृत्युक्लेशादयस्तथा।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मिन्नादिपञ्चवर्गञ्च ज्ञात्वा ब्रूयात्पुरोक्तितः॥१४५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Saturn is in Taurus, he is thinking about a buffalo; if Saturn is in Libra, the idea is about a man with a wheel; if Saturn is in Scorpio, he is thinking of illness; if Saturn is in Aries, he is thinking of death and pain.Along with these, the astrologist has to take into consideration these five categories of a planet's friend, exaltation, own house, neutral and enemy; he has to give predictions in accordance with what is stated in verses 127 and 128. 145  

**धातुराशौ धातुखगैर्दृष्टे तच्छत्रसंयुते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**धातुचिन्ता भवेत्तद्वन्मूलजीवौ तथा वदेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**धातुभस्थे मूलखेटे जीवमाहुर्विपश्चितः॥१४६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Dhaatu Raasis (Aries, Cancer, Libra and Capricom) are aspected by Dhaatu planets (Mars, the Moon and Saturn) or become Chhatra Raasis, the thought is stated to be about Dhaatus. The same is the case with Moola Raasis and Jeeva Raasis too; *i.e*. if they are aspected by Moola or Jeeva Raasis respectively or become Chhatra Raasis. Some pandits affirm that even if Moola planets (the Sun and Venus) are in Dhaatu Raasis, they are stated to be Jeevas. 146

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**जीवराशौ मूलखगैर्दृष्टे वा युजि मूलकाः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मूलराशौजीवखगैर्धातुचिन्ता प्रकीर्तिता॥१४७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Jeeva Raasis are aspected by Moola, planets or associated with them, the thought is only about Moolas. If the Moola Raasis are aspected by the Jeeva planets, or associated with them, the thought is about Dhaatu products. 147

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**त्रिवर्गखेटकैः दृष्टे युक्ते बलवशाद्वदेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पश्यन्ति चन्द्रञ्चेदन्ये वदेत्तत्तद्ग्रहाकृतिम्॥१४८॥**  

 As stated above, if the three kinds of Raasis Dhaatu Moola and Jeeva are aspected by or associated with any of the three kinds of planets, Dhaatu, Moola or Jeeva, prediction about the idea thought about should be made after considering the strength of the various planets. If other planets aspect the Moon, the size of the planets (as stated in verses 68 & 69) is to be considered and their respective products predicted. 148

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**धातुं मूलञ्च जीवञ्च वंशं वर्णं स्मृतं वदेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदयारूढयोश्छत्रे ग्रहयोगेक्षणात्तथा॥१४९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 One has to take into consideration the qualities and attributes of the rising sign, the Aaroodha Raasi, and the sign where the Moon is posited and the nature of the planets associated with or aspecting these. Then prediction is to be made in respect of the idea thought about in terms of Dhaatu, Moola, Jeeva, caste colour etc. described in verses 97 to 101. 149

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ज्ञात्वा नष्टञ्च मुष्टिञ्च चिन्तनां क्रमशो वदेत्। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कण्टकादिचतुष्के तु स्वोत्वमित्रग्रहैर्युते। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**दृष्टे वा सर्वकार्याणां सिद्धिं ब्रूयाच्च चिन्तिताम्॥ १५०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदये धातुचिन्ता स्यादारूढे मूलचिन्तनम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**छत्रेषु जीवचिन्ता स्यादिति कैश्चिदुदाहृतम्॥१५१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**केन्द्रं पणफरं प्रोक्तमापोक्लिममिति क्रमात्। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चिन्तनामुष्टिनष्टानि कथयेत्कार्यसिद्धये॥१५२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The loss of an article, the hidden article in the fist or the idea thought about are to be predicted thus; If the planets are in quadrants (the 1st, 4th, 7th and 10th places) and if the planets are in their own houses, or in. friendly signs or in exaltation or if they aspect the quadrants (the 1st, 4th, 7th and 10th places; the desired result will come into effect. From the rising Lagna, all ideas about Dhaatus from Aaroodha Lagna and thoughts about Moola and from Chhatra Raasi everything about Jeeva can be predicted. By studying the quadrants (the 1st, 4th, 7th and 10th houses) the idea thought about can be predicted by studying the Panapharas (the 2nd, 5th, 8th and 11th houses), the article hidden in the fist can be stated, by studying the Aapoklimas (the 3rd, 9th, 6th and 12th places) the loss of an article can be traced from these, the success of the venture can be determined.  
 From verse 122 to verse 152 the methods of determining the loss of property or the idea thought about are detailed, and one has to apply them appropriately as the occasion demands before prediction. 150–152 
                                   
                            

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681983526.png)  
**Chapter VI**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***ON AAROODHA***

</div>



<div>


**तत आरूढगे चन्द्रे न नष्टं रुद्धशाश्वती।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आरूढाद्दशमे वृद्धिञ्चतुर्थे पूर्ववद्वदेत्।  
नष्टद्रव्यस्य लाभश्व सर्वहानिश्च सप्तमे॥१५३॥**  

 If the Moon is in the Aaroodha Raasi, there is no loss of property; it is only hidden from sight for the time being; it is indestructible and can be found.  
 If the Moon is in the 10th house from the Aaroodha Lagna there will be increase of profit; if it is in the 4th house, the prediction is as stated earlier, *i.e.* lost property can be recovered but if it is in the 7th house, loss of property is to be predicted. 153

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**उदयाद्वादशे षष्ठेऽष्टम आरूढके सति।  
चिन्तितार्थो न भवति धनहानिर्द्विषद्वलम्॥१५४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the rising Lagna is either in the 12th, 8th or 6th house from Aaroodha Lagna, the lost property cannot be recovered. In addition to financial loss, the enemy will be strengthened. 154

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तनुं कुटुम्बं सहजं जननीं तनयं रिपुम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कलत्रं निधनं चैव गुरुं कर्म फलं व्ययम्। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदयादिक्रमाद्भावं तस्य तस्य फलं वदेत्॥१५५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The respective effects of the position of the rising Lagna, in relation to the Aaroodha Lagna are as follows: in the first house, it is related to the body; in the 2nd, family; in the 3rd, brothers; in the 4th, mother; in the 5th, children; in the 6th, enemy; in the 7th, spouse; in the 8th, death; in the 9th, perceptor; in the 10th, work; in the 11th, gain; and in the 12th expenses. 155

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**रवीन्दुशुक्रजीवज्ञा नृराशिषु यदा स्थिताः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मर्त्यचिन्ता ततः सौरिदृष्टे नष्टं कुजे तथा।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कुजस्य कलहः सौरेस्तस्करं गरलं वदेत्॥१५६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Sun, the Moon, Venus, Jupiter and Mercury are male Raasis, the idea thought about is men; if the rising Lagna is aspected by Saturn and has relations with Mars, the idea is about lost property; if the rising Lagna is only having relation with Mars, the idea is about strife or conflict; if it is only aspected by Satum, the idea is about thieves or poisoning. 156

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**रविदृष्टे तथायुक्ते चिन्तना देवभूपयोः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुभचिन्ता गुरौ ज्ञेया विवाहो बुधशुक्रयोः॥१५७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the rising Lagna is either associated with or aspected by the Sun, the idea in the enquirer's mind is about a king or god; if aspected by or associated with Jupiter, the idea is about noble and good things; and if associated with or aspected by Mercury or Venus, the person is thinking about marriage matters. 157

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681983526.png)  
**Chapter VII**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***ON CHHATRA RAASI***

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**द्वितीये द्वादशे छत्रे सर्वं कार्यं विनश्यति।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**गुरौ पश्यति युक्ते वा तत्र कार्यं शुभं वदेत्॥१५८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Chhatra Raasi is in the 2nd place or the 12th place to Prasna Lagna or Aaroodha Lagna, all undertakings will fail. But if Jupiter is in Chhatra Raasi or aspects it, all work will be successful. 158

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**तृतीयैकादशे छत्रे सर्वं कार्यं शुभं वदेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तस्मिन्पापयुते दृष्टे विषयं भवति ध्रुवम्॥१५९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Chhatra Raasi is in the 3rd or 11th place to Prasna Lagna or Aaroodha Lagna all undertakings will be successful. But if a malefic is posited in or aspects the Chhatra Raasi there will be certain failure of any work undertaken. 159

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**तस्मिन्सौम्ययुते दृष्टे सर्वं कार्यं शुभं वदेत्। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मिश्रे मिश्रफलं ब्रूयाच्छास्त्रे ज्ञानप्रदीपके॥१६०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If a benefic planet is posited in or aspects the Chhatra Raasi all enterprises will meet with success. If both benefic and malefic planets have connection with the Chhatra Raasi,the science of Pragnaana Pradeepikaa teaches that the results will be of mixed nature. 160

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पञ्चमे नवमे छत्रे सर्वसिद्धिर्भविष्यति।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तद्वच्छुभाशुभैर्दृष्टे मिश्र मिश्रफलं भवेत्॥१६१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Chhatra Raasi happens to be the 5th or the 9th sign all undertakings will be successful. If it is associated with a benefic planet, success will corne; and if with a malefic planet failure would be the result. But if both malefic and benefic planets are there, the result will be of a mixed character. 161

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**द्वितीये चाष्टमे षष्ठे द्वादशे छत्रसंयुते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नष्टद्रव्यागमो नास्ति न व्याधिशमनं भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**न कार्यसिद्धिर्नद्वेषशान्तिर्गृहवशाद्भवेत्॥१६२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Chhatra Raasi is in the 2nd, 8th, 6th or 12th house, the lost property cannot be recovered; diseases also will not be cured; the wished for fruit cannot be attained; and enmity will not cease. 162

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681808575.png)  
**Chapter VIII*  
**ON THE RISING RAASI***

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**वृहस्पत्युदये श्रेयो धनं विजय आगमः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**द्वेषशान्तिस्सर्वकार्यसिद्धिरेव न संशयः॥१६३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Jupiter is posited in the rising Raasi, good will result; more property and victory wiill come; ill–will and enmity die; and all enterprises will certainly succeed. 163

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**सौम्योदये रणोद्योगी जित्वा तद्धनमाहरेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पुनरेष्यति सिद्धिस्स्याच्चन्द्रसन्दर्शने तथा।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**व्यवहारे च विजयश्छत्रे प्येवमुदाहृतम्॥१६४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Mercury is in the rising Raasi, the warrior will defeat his foe and come back with the ( victor's) spoils. If the Moon aspects the rising Raasi, the man who goes out to accomplish a work will come back with achievement, he will succeed in litigation. The same good result will be there if Jupiter, Mercury and the Moon are in Chhatra Raasi. 164

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**चन्द्रोदयेऽर्थलाभश्वोपायेनागमनन्तथा।  
चिन्तितार्थस्य लाभश्च छत्रारूढस्थितेपि च॥१६५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Moon is posited in Udaya (rising) Raasi, the person will gain property by many ways and get his desiredends. The same prediction can be given if the Moon is in Chhatra Raasi or Aaroodha Raasi. 165

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुक्रोदयेऽर्थसिद्धिस्स्यात् स्त्रीलाभो व्याधिमोचनम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चयो यान्त्यरयस्स्नेहं छत्रेप्येवमुदाहृतम्॥१६६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Venus is in Udaya Raasi, there will be gain in property, acquisition of woman, curing of illness, victory and friendliness with erst–while foes. The same will happen if Venus is in Chhatra Raasi. 
166

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदयारूढछत्रेषु शन्यर्काङ्गारका यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अर्थनाशं मनस्तापं मरणं व्याधिमादिशेत्॥१६७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Saturn, the Sun or Mars is in Udaya, Chhatra or Aaroodha Raasi, there will be loss of property, ill–will and unfriendliness, illness and death.                                
               167

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**एतेषु फणियुर्क्तेषु बन्धं चोरभयं गरम्।  
मरणं चैव दैवज्ञो न सन्दिग्धो वदेत्सुधीः॥१६८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Rahu is associated with the Udaya, Chhatra or Aaroodha Raasi, there will be bondage, fear of thieves, poisoning and even death. 168

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**निधनारिभ्रनस्थेषु पापेष्वशुभमादिशेत्।  
एषु स्थानेषु केन्द्रेषु शुभास्स्युश्चेच्छुभं वदेत्॥१६९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If malefics are in the 2nd, 9th or 8th places, misery is to be predicted. But if benefics are posited in those places or in Kendras, prosperity is to be predicted. 169

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**तन्वादिभावः पापैस्तु युक्तो दृष्टो विनश्यति।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुभैर्युक्ते च दृष्टे च तत्तद्भावाभिपोषणम्॥१७०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If maleflcs are posited in or aspecting the Lagnas, namely Udaya, Chhatra or Aaroodha destruction will result. But if benefics are posited in or aspecting these Lagnas, good willaccrue. 170

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


![](../books_images/1681809651.png)

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

**Chapter IX**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***ABOUT LOST PROPERTY***

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**तुलोदये क्रियारूढे नष्टसिद्धिर्न संशयः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**विपरीते न नष्टाप्तिर्वृषारूढेऽलिभोदये।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नष्टसिद्धिर्महालाभो विपरीते विपर्ययः॥१७१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Libra is Udaya Raasi and Aries the Aaroodha Raasi, the loss of property will certainly be recovered. If it is the reverse, i.e. Aries is Udaya Raasi and Libra the Aaroodha Raasi, the property cannot be recovered.  
If Scorpio is Udaya Raasi and Taurus the Aaroodha Raasi not only will the lost property be recovered but additional gains will accrue. If it is otherwise, *i.e.* Scorpio, the Aaroodha Raasi and Taurus the Udaya Raasi, the lost property cannot be regained. 171

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चापारूढे नष्टसिद्धिर्भविता मिथुनोदये।  
विपरीते न सिद्धिस्स्यात्कर्कारूढे मृगोदये। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सिद्धिश्च विपरीते तु न सिद्ध्यति न संशयः॥१७२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Gemini is Udaya Raasi and Sagittarius the Aaroodha Raasi one can regain the lost property. In the reyerse case, the lost property cannot be traced. If Capricom is AaroodhaRaasi and Cancer the Udaya Raasi, "there will be success in the venture. In the reverse case, *i.e.* Cancer the Aaroodha and Capricom Udaya Raasi, failure will be the result. 172

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**सिह्मोदये घटारूढे नष्टसिद्धिर्न संशयः। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**विपरीते न सिद्धिस्स्याज्झषारूढेङ्गनोदये। **

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नष्टसिद्धिर्विपर्यासे दृष्टादृष्टे निरूपयेत्॥१७३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Leo is Udaya Raasi and Aquarius the Aoroodha Raasi, there will be certainty of regaining lost property. In the reverse case of Leo being Aaroodha and Aquarius the Udaya Raasi, one cannot regain the property. If Virgo is Udaya Raasi and Pisces Aaroodha there will be success in regaining the property. In the reverse case of Virgo the Aaroodha and Pisces Udaya, failure will be the result. 173

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्थिरोदये स्थिरारूढे स्थिरच्छत्रं भवेद्यदि।  
न मृतिर्नच नष्टञ्च न रोगशमनं तथा॥१७४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Udaya, Aaroodha and Chhatra are in fixed Raasis, and the enquirer asks about death, there will be no death; if he asks about lost property, he will get back that property; and if he asks about illness, he will not be cured of it. 174

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**द्विदेहभोदयारूढे छत्रे नष्टं न सिद्ध्यति।  
न व्याधिशमनं शत्रोत्सन्धिं विद्यान्नचस्थिराम्॥१७५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Udaya, Aaroodha and Chhatra are in common Raasis, and the querist asks about lost property, he will not get back that property; if about illness, it will not be cured; and if about enmity, the truce arrived at between the parties cannot last long. 175

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चरराश्युदयारूढछत्रेषु स्त्र्यादिसिद्धयः।  
नष्टसिद्धिश्च भवति व्याधिशान्तिश्च जायते॥१७६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Udaya, Aaroodha and Chhatra are in moveable Raasis, there will certainly he success in all fields; gain of a woman, recovery of lost property, curing of diseases, and accomplishment of all enterprises undertaken. 176  

**सर्वागमनकार्याणि भवन्त्येव न संशयः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ग्रहस्थितिबलेनैव सर्वं ब्रूयाच्छुभाशुभम्।  
चरोदये स्थितास्सौम्यास्सर्वकार्यार्थसाधकाः॥१७७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Good or bad results are to be predicted by proper assessment of the strength of the various planets in the different Raasis. If the Udaya Lagna is in moveable Raasis and benefic planets are posited therein, all kinds of work undertaken will succeed. 177

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आरूढछत्रलग्नेषु क्रूरेष्वस्तङ्गतेषु च।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**परेणापहृतं ब्रूयात्तत्सिद्ध्यति शुभेषु च॥१७८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If malefics or eclipsed planets are posited in Aaroodha, Udaya or Chhatra Raasis, the lost property must have been taken away by some one and no hope is there of recovery. But if benefics are there, hope of recovery can be predicted. 178  

**नवमे पञ्चमेस्ते च नष्टलाभः शुभोदये।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**एषु पापे न नष्टाप्तिरुदयादित्रिकेषु च॥१७९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If benefics are in the 5th, 7th or 9th place from Aaroodha, Udaya or Chhatra Raasi, the lost property can be recovered. By determining the condition of the planets, benefic or malefic, weak or strong, in the Udaya, Aaroodha or Chhatra Raasis, the possibility of recovery or otherwise of lost property can be predicted. 179

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**भ्रातृस्थानयुते पापे पञ्चमे वाशुभेक्षिते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नष्टद्रव्याणि केनापि दीयन्ते स्वयमेव च॥१८०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If even a malefic is in the 3rd house or a benefic in the 5th house from the Udaya, Aaroodha or ChhatraRaasi the man who has taken the property will, of his own accord, return it. 180  

**प्रश्नकाले शुभेपापे धूमेन परिवेष्टिते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नष्टं नष्टे न भवति तत्तदाशासु तिष्ठति॥१८१॥**

</div>

 If a benefic or a malefic planet is associated with the Upagraha Dhooma at the time of Prasna the alleged lost property is not lost but is intact in the direction indicated by the planet. 181

<div>


**पृष्ठोदये शशाङ्के तु नष्टद्रव्यं न गच्छति।**

</div>

<div>

**तद्राशिश्शनिदृष्टश्चेन्नष्टं व्योम्नि कुजे न तत्॥१८२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If at the time of Prasna the Moon is in the Prishthodaya sign (Arics, Taurus, Cancer, Sagittarius or Capricorn) the alleged 'lost' property is not lost but is somewhere in the house itself. If that sign is aspected by Saturn the article is in a high place, and if that sign has any relation with Mars it is not in the high place. 182  

**वृहस्पत्युदये स्वर्णे नष्टं नास्तीति निर्दिशेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**शुक्रे चतुर्थगे रौप्यं नष्टं न भवति धूवम्॥१८३॥**

</div>

 If Jupiter is in the Udaya Lagna, the lost property is a golden article, but really it is not lost; if Venus is in the 4th place from Udaya Lagna, the alleged lost article is a silver one, and really it is not lost. 183

<div>

**अस्ते कुजे शनौ कृष्णलोहं नष्टं न जायते।**

</div>

<div>

**वुधोदये त्रपु प्रायो नष्टं नास्ति चतुर्थगे॥१८४॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Saturn or Mars is in the 7th place, the lost article is an iron one, and it is not lost; if Mercury is in the UdayaRaasi or in the 4th place from it, the lost article is a tin or zinc one, and it is not lost. 184

</div>

<div>


**कांस्यं नष्टं न भवति पङ्कनाभौ च सप्तमे।**

</div>

<div>

**आरकूटं पञ्चमस्थे भानौ नष्टं न जायते॥१८५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Moon is in the 7th place, the lost article is a bronze one and really it is not lost; If the Sun is in the 5th place, the lost article is made of brass and really it is not lost. 185  

**दशमे पापसंयुक्ते न नष्टाश्च चतुष्पदाः।  
चतुष्पदोदये राहौ स्थिते नष्टाश्चतुष्पदाः॥१८६॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If malefics are associated in the 10th place, the lost one is an animal and really it is not lost; and if the Udaya Raasi is a quadruped sign and Rahu is posited therein, the animal is to be considered as lost. 186

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**बन्धनस्था भवेयुस्ते तद्वद्विपदराशयः।  
बहुपादुदये राहौ बहुपान्नष्टिमादिशेत्।  
पक्षिराशौ पदा नष्टमेतेषां बन्धनं भवेत्॥१८७॥**  

If the Udaya Raasi is a biped sign and if Rahu is posited therein a human being is in jail (or in bondage) and if the Udaya Raasi is a multifooted sign and if Rahu is posited there the animal is lost. If the Udaya Raasi is a bird signand Rahu is there, the above predictions have to be stated namely, that the man will be in jail and the animal in the pound. 187

</div>

<div>


**कर्कवृश्चिकयोर्लग्ने नष्टं सद्मनि कीर्तयेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**मृगमीनोदये नष्टं कपोतान्तरयोर्वदेत्॥१८८॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

 If Cancer or Scorpio is the Udaya Lagna, the lost article is in a loft or in the middle of the house. 188

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**कलशे भूमिजस्सौम्यो घटे रक्तघटे गुरुः।  
शुक्रश्च करके लग्ने घटे भास्करनन्दनः॥१८९॥**

</div>

<div>


**आरनालघटे भाण्डे चन्द्रो लवणभाण्डके।**

</div>

<div>

**नष्टद्रव्याश्रितं स्थानं सद्मनीति विनिर्दिशेत्॥१९०॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Mars is in the Udaya Lagna, the lost article will be in a pot; if it is Mercury it is certainly in a pot; if it is Jupiter the article is in a red–clay pot; and if it is Venus, it is in the water jug; and if it is Saturn the article is in rice–cleansed water; and if it is the Moon the article will be in the salt jug. 189–190

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**पुंराशिः पुङग्रहैर्दृष्टः पुरुषस्तस्करो भवेत्।  
स्त्रीराशिः स्त्रीग्रहैदृष्टः तस्करी च वधूर्भवेत्॥१९१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If male Raasis are aspected by male planets, the thief is a man. Likewise if female Raasis are aspected by female planets, the thief is a woman. 191

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**उदयादोजराशिस्थे पुङ्ग्रहे पुरुषो भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**समराश्युदये चोरी समस्थे स्त्रीग्रहे वधूः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदयारूढयोश्चैव बलाबलवशाद्वदेत्॥१९२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If from the Udaya Raasi a male planet is in an odd number sign the thief is a man. If the Udaya Raasi is an even number sign, and if from that a female planet is in an even sigin the thief is a woman. What is stated is to be considered in the light of the strength of the Udaya and Aaroodha signs. 192

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कर्किनक्रपुरन्ध्रीषु नष्टद्रव्यं न सिध्यति।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तुलाबृषभकुम्भेषु नष्टद्रव्यं च सिध्यति।  
जीवं विना सर्वखगे सपत्नस्थे न सिध्यति॥१९३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Cancer, Capricorn and Virgo are the Udaya signs, the lost property cannot be recovered. If Libra, Taurus and Aquarius are the Udaya signs, the lost property can be restored. Excepting Jupiter if any other planet is in an inimical sign, the lost article cannot be obtained. 196

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पश्यन्ति ये ग्रहाश्चन्द्रं चोरास्तत्तुल्यरूपिणः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**द्रव्याणि च तथैव स्युरिति ज्ञात्वा वदेत्सुधीः॥१९४॥**

</div>

<div>


 Whatever planet aspects the Moon, the thief will havethe features of that planet. The stolen article too will have some semblance to that planet. 194

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**यस्यामारूढभं याति तस्यां दिशि गतं वदेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**तत्तद्ग्रहांशुसङ्ख्यानि तत्तत्सङ्ख्यादिनादिकम्।**

</div>

<div>

**स्वभावकवशादेव मन्यदृष्टिंवशाद्वदेत्॥१९५॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 The lost article will be in that direction in which the Aaroodha sign is situated. The time taken to recover the lost property can be reckoned in terms of days according to the rays of the planets concerned, or the months and years of the planets according to the circumstances of the case. Accordingly prediction is to be made taking into consideration the nature of the planets and of those aspecting the Aaroodha, Udaya and Chhatra signs. 195

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**चन्द्रस्थर्क्षादुदयभं यावत्तावत्फलं वदेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**चरस्थिरोभयवशादेकद्वित्रिगुणो भवेत्॥१९६॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

The number of signs separating the Udaya Raasi from the house in which the Moon is situated gives the number of days by which success will be effected. If the signs of the Moon and the Udaya Lagna are moveable signs, the above number gives the days for fruition of the prediction. If they are fixed signs, the number has to be trebled. 196

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681811435.png)  
**Chapter X**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***OF GAIN AND LOSS***

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**सुवस्तुलाभं राज्यञ्च राष्ट्रलाभं स्त्रियः पतिम्।**

</div>

<div>

**उपायनं स्वकार्याणां लाभालाभौ वदेत्सुधीः॥१९७॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**उदयादित्रिकान्खेटाः पश्यन्त्युश्चेश्वरा यदि।**

</div>

<div>

**चिन्तितार्थागमाश्चैव स्त्रीलाभो राज्यसिद्धयः॥१९८॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**तान्नीचद्वेषिणो खेटाः पश्यन्ति यदि नाशयेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**एवं विवाहकार्येच शुभाशुभनिरूपणम्॥१९९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If planets in exaltation aspect the Udaya, Aaroodha or Chhatra signs, gain of valuable goods, even of, kingdoms is to be predicted. For females, gain of a husband, rewards, achievement of tasks undertaken and obtaining of desired things can be predicted. For males, gaining a wife and obtaining a job will be predicted by wise men. If however planets in debilitation or inimical planets aspect the Udaya, Aaroodha or Chhatra signs the reverse of the above predictions is indicated. That is, there will be loss all around. Likewise, prediction is to be made regarding marriage. 197–199

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**उदयारूढछत्राणि पश्यन्ति सुहृदो यदि।**

</div>

<div>

**शत्रुर्मित्रत्वमायाति रिपुः पश्यति चेद्रिपुः॥२००॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the lords of the Udaya, Aaroodha and Chhatra signs are aspected by benefic planets, even an enemy will become a friend. If however, malefic planets aspect them, even a friend will become an enemy. 200

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**उदयञ्चन्द्रलग्नञ्च रिपुः पश्यति वा युतः।  
आयुर्हानी रिपुस्थानं गतश्चेद्बन्धनं भवेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**गतो न यदि नष्टञ्चेब्दहिरेव गतं वदेत्॥२०१॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If a malefic planet either occupies or aspects the Udaya Lagna or the Moon's sign, there will be decline in longevity; if they occupy an inimical sign, there will be bondage (*i.e.* imprisonment). If the Moon does not reach an inimical sign, the lost property has been taken out. 201

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**बलवच्चन्द्रजीवाभ्यां केन्द्रेषु सहितेषु च।**

</div>

<div>

**नष्टप्रश्नेन नष्टं स्यात् मृत्युप्रश्नेन नश्यति।**

</div>

<div>

**पापदृष्टे युते केन्द्रे ब्रूयात्तस्य विपर्ययम्॥२०२॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If a strong Moon or Jupiter is in Kendra and a query is asked at that time, if it is with regard to loss of property, prediction can be made that there is no loss. If it is about death, it can safely be said that there will be no death. Ifhowever, malefics are either posited in or aspecting the Kendras, the reverse prediction is to be made *i.e.* the property cannot be recovered, and death may take place. 202

</div>

<div>


**शत्रोरागमनं नास्ति चतुर्थे पापसंयुते।  
दशमैकादशे सौम्यग्रहाश्चेत्सर्वसिद्धयः॥२०३॥**

</div>

<div>


 If malefics are in the 4th place, the enemy dare not come. If benefics are in the 10th an 11th places, all enterprises undertaken will be successful. 203

</div>

<div>


**उदयारूढछत्रेषु केन्द्रेषु भुजगो यदि।**

</div>

<div>

**दूरस्थितो नचाऽऽयाति बद्धो भविष्यति॥२०४॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Rahu is posited in Udaya, Aaroodha and Chhatra Paasis or in their trines, the person who has gone far away from home will not return. He may be in bondage there. 204

</div>

<div>


**विषादिपीडा प्रश्नेतु रोगिणो मरणं भवेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**गमनं विद्यते प्रष्टुर्नास्तीति कथयेद्बुधः।**

</div>

<div>

**प्रारब्धकार्यहानिस्स्याद्धनस्यापत्तिरीरिता॥२०५॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If in the above case, questions relating to poison are asked, the person will die. The enquirer would go to the place where the person is confined, but his presence wouldbe of no avail; there would be loss of property and all undertakings would fail. 205

</div>

<div>


**चन्द्राद्व्योमस्थिते शुक्रे जीवाद्व्योमस्थिते रवौ**

</div>

<div>

**तल्लग्ने कार्यसिद्धिस्स्यात्पृच्छकानां न संशयः॥२०६॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Venus is in the 10th place from the Moon and if the Sun is in the 10th place from Jupiter at the time of Prasna all kinds of work undertaken by the enquirer would succeed. 206

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**उदयात्सप्तमे व्योम्नि शुक्रश्चेत्स्त्रीसमागमः।**

</div>

<div>

**धनागमश्च सौख्यञ्च चन्द्रेऽप्येवं प्रकीर्तितम्॥२०७॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Venus is in the 7th or 10th place from the Udaya Lagna, there will be conjugal bliss, addition to wealth and prosperity. The same good results will accrue if the Moon is in the 7th or 10th place from the Udaya Lagna. 207

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**मित्रस्वात्युच्चमायान्ति यदा खेटास्तदेष्टदाः।**

</div>

<div>

**नीचारिबलयोगाभ्यां सर्वकार्यविनाशनम्॥२०८॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 When the planets reach their friend's house, or are in own house or in very high exaltation then they confer all good benefits; and when they are in debilitation or in their enemy's house, all kinds of work will meet with failure. 208

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681812026.png)

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

**ChapterXI**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***ON DISEASES***

</div>

<div>


**पूर्वशास्त्रानुसारेण व्याधिमृत्युविनिर्णयः।**

</div>

<div>

**षष्ठो य उदयाद्व्याधिरष्टमो मृत्युसंज्ञकः।  
तत्र षष्ठे व्याधिचिन्ता निधने मृत्युचिन्तना॥२०९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 Predictions about diseases and death are made in terms of the Saastraic rules. The 6th sign from Udaya Lagna indicates disease, and the 8th sign, death. 209

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**तत्तदूग्रहयुते दृष्टे व्याधिं मृत्युं वदेक्रमात्।**

</div>

<div>

**पापनीचारयः खेटाः पश्यन्ति यदिसंयुताः।  
न व्याधिशमनं मृत्युं प्रविचार्य वदेत्सुधीः॥२१०॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Whatever planets are in association with or aspecting the 6th and 8th signs, predictions regarding diseases and death are to be made. Even if malefics or debilitated planets or inimical planets are posited in or aspecting the 6th; and 8th houses, diseases would not be cured, nor death prevented. 210

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**एतयोश्चन्द्रभुजगौ तिष्ठतो यदि चोदये।  
गरादिना भवेद्व्याधिर्नशाम्यति न संशयः।**

</div>

<div>

**पृष्ठोदयर्क्षे तच्छत्रे व्याधिमोक्षो न जायते॥२११॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Moon or Rahu is in Udaya Lagna or in the 6th or 8th house, disease will occur due to poisoning or witchcraft but will not be cured. Even if the Moon sign in Udaya Lagna is in Prishthodaya Raasi, the illness will not be cured. 211

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**व्याधिस्थानमिदं प्राहुर्मूर्ध्नि वक्त्रे भुजे करे।**

</div>

<div>

**वक्षसि स्तनयोः कुक्षौ कक्षे मूले च मेहने।  
ऊरौ पादौ च मेषाद्या राशयः परिकीर्तिताः॥२१२॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 In terms of the bodily organs, Aries is regarded as the head, Taurus the face, Gemini the arms, Cancer the hands, Leo the chest, Virgo the breasts, Libra the stomach, Scorpio the armpits, Sagittarius the arms, Capricorn the genitals, Aquarius the thighs, and Pisces the legs. In terms of the signs, the affected parts of the body can be predicted. 212

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**कुजो मूर्ध्नि मुखे शुक्रः कण्ठे राहुर्भुजे वुधः। **

</div>

<div>

**चन्द्रो वक्षसि कुक्षौ च भानुर्नाभेरधो गुरुः। **

</div>

<div>

**ऊरौ शनिरहिः पादे ग्रहाणां स्थानमीरितम्॥२१३॥**  


</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 In terms of the planets, the bodily organs are distributed thus; Mars is the head, Venus the face, Rahu the neck, Mercury the arms, the Moon the chest, the Sun the stomach, Jupiter the lower portion below the navel, Saturn the thighs, and Ketu the feet. 213

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**एतेष्वेव स्थलेषु स्यान्नष्टमेतेषु राशिषु।**

</div>

<div>

**पावयुक्तेषु दृष्टेषु नीचारिस्थेषु रुग्भवेद्॥२१४॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If at the time of Prasna any sign is rising in the horizon, the lost property will be in the place assigned to that sign. Likewise, if malefics are posited in or aspecting or, if weak or inimical planets are in any sign, the corresponding parts of the body in terms of the sign and planet will be affected by disease. 214

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**पश्यन्ति ये ग्रहाश्चन्द्रं व्याधिस्थानावलोकिनम्।**

</div>

<div>

**पूर्वोक्तमासवर्षाणि दिनानि च वदेद्बुधः॥२१५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The time taken for cure of the illness will be in terms of the days, months, and years of the planets (given in verses 84 and 85) aspecting the Moon which sees the oth house. 215

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**षष्ठाष्टमे पापयुते रोगशान्तिर्न जायते।**

</div>

<div>

**षष्ठाष्टमे शुभयुते तदा व्याधिविमोचनम्॥२१६॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If malefics are posited in the 6th and 8th houses from the Udaya Lagna, the disease will not be cured. But if, however, benefics are there, the disease will be cured. 216

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**किञ्चिदत्र विशेषोऽस्ति रोगमृत्युस्थिते शुभाः।**

</div>

<div>

**यावद्भिर्दिवसैर्यन्ति तावद्भिर्व्याधिमोचनम्॥२१७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 But there is one special feature to be noted. The time taken for cure of the illness will be the number of days taken by the benefics to transit the 6th and 8th houses. 217

</div>

<div>


**रोगस्थानाद्भवेऽस्ते वा पापखेटयुते तथा।**

</div>

<div>

**षष्ठाष्टमे चन्द्रयुते मरणं रोगिणां भवेत्॥२१८॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If at the time of Prasna, malefics are in the 7th or 11th place from the 6th house (called the house of illness), or if the Moon is posited in the 6th or 8th house, death is certain. 218

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**रोगस्थानं कुजः पश्येच्छिरस्तोदो ज्वरो भवेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**भृगुविषूचिस्सौम्यश्चेत् कक्षे ग्रन्थिर्भविष्यति॥२२०॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Mars aspects the house of illness (the 6th place), the person will have headache and fever. If Venus aspects it, he will get cholera; it Mercury aspects it, he will get boils in his armpits. 219

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**रविश्चेदुदरव्याधिः शनिर्वातश्च पङ्गुता।**

</div>

<div>

**राहुर्विषं शशी पश्येन्नेत्ररोगो भविष्यति॥२२०॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Sun aspects the house of illness (the 6th), the person will suffer from stomach–ache; If Saturn aspects it he will have wind–diseases or become lame; If Rahu aspects it, he will suffer from poisoning; and if the Moon aspects it,he will have eye–affliction. If Jupiter aspects it, he will have piles; and the effects of Venus will be like that of the Moon, say some. 220

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**मूलव्याधिः गुरुः पश्येज्वन्द्रवत्स्याद् भृगुः परे।**

</div>

<div>

**परिघाविन्द्रकोदण्डदृष्टे प्रश्न ते सति।**

</div>

<div>

**कुष्ठव्याधिमिति ब्रूयाद्धूमे भूताहतं वदेत्। २२१॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If at the time of Prasna, the Upagraha Indradhanus aspects or associates with the Parivesha ("another Upagraha), the person will be afflicted by leprosy. If Indradhanus associates with or aspects the Dhoomagraha (another subplanet), the person will be tormented by ghosts and devils. 221

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**सर्वेऽपस्मारमादित्ये पिशाचपरिपीडनम्।  
काशं श्वासं च शूलं च शनौ शीतज्वरः कुजे॥२२२॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Indradhanus is associated with or aspects.any planet, the person will suffer from epilepsy; and if the Sun is aspected by or associated with Indradhanus, affliction by ghosts is to be predicted. If Saturn is afflicted by Indradhanus, either by association or aspect, the person will suffer from consumption; and Mars is similarly affected, the person will suffer from malaria. 222

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**शुक्रे कोदण्डपरिधिदृष्टे प्रश्नेतु रोगिणाम्।**

</div>

<div>

**न व्याधिशमनं किञ्चिद्यदि नेक्षन्ति चेच्छुभाः।**

</div>

<div>

**रोगशान्तिर्भवेच्छीघ्रं मित्रस्वात्युच्च संस्थिताः॥२२३॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If at the time of Prasna, Venus is aspected by the sub–planets Indradhanus and Praivesha and not by any benefic, there will be no cure of the disease. But if a benefic is in a friendly house, own house, or in very high exaltation, the disease will be cured very soon. 223

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**शिरोललाटभ्रूनेत्रनासिकाश्रुतयोऽधरः।**

</div>

<div>

**चुबुकञ्चाङ्गुलिश्चैव कृत्तिकाद्या नवोडवः॥२२४॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If at the time of the Prasna, anyone of the following nine stars is rising in the horizon – Krittikaa, Rohini, Mrigasira, Aardraa, Punarvasu, Pushyami, Aasleshaa, Makha and Pubba, the parts of the body afflicted will be respectively head, forehead, brow, eye, nose, ear, lower lip, chin, and finger. 224

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**कण्ठवक्षःस्थलकुचोदरमध्यनितम्बकाः।  
शिश्रमण्डोऽधरः प्रोक्तश्चोत्तराद्या नवोडवः॥२२५॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the next nine stars are rising, namely, Uttaraa, Hasta, Chittaa, Swaatee, Visaakhaa, Anuraadhaa, Jyeshthaa, Moolaa and Poorvaashaadhaa, the afflicted parts arerespectively, neck, chest, breast, stomach, waist, buttocks, genital, the scrotum, and the upper lip. 225

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**जानुजङ्घापादसन्धि पृष्ठान्तः स्फिचगुल्फकाः।**

</div>

<div>

**पादाग्रतालिकाङ्गुल्यो विश्वर्क्षाद्या नवोडवः॥२२६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If at the time of Prasna, the final nine stars are rising–Uttaraashaadhaa, Sravana, Dhanishtaa, Satabhisha, Poorvabhadra, Uttarabhadra, Revatee, Aswinee and Bharanee, the affected parts of the body are knee, calf, ankle, groin, back of the thighs, heel, and toes. 226

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**उदयर्क्षवशादेवं ज्ञात्वा तत्र गदं वदेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**अर्कनक्षत्रकं ज्ञात्वा नष्टद्रव्यं तथा वदेत्॥२२७॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

 From the stars, the respective affected parts can be predicted as above. Finding the star near the Sun the lostarticle can also be predicted. 227

</div>

<div>


**त्रिकोणलग्नदशमे शुभश्चेद्व्याधयो नहि।**

</div>

<div>

**तेषु नीचारियुक्तेषु देहपीडा भविष्यति॥२२८॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If a benefic occupies Trikona, Lagna or the 10th house, diseases will not afflict. If the planet is debilitated or inimical, disease will afflict. 228

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681818159.png)  
**Chapter XII**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***ON DEATH***

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**मरणस्य विधानानि ज्ञातव्यानि मनीषिभिः।**

</div>

<div>

**वृषस्य वृषभश्छत्रं सिह्मश्छत्रं हरेर्भवेत्॥२२९॥**

</div>

<div>


 Wise men can predict the time of death as in the following: 229

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**अलिनो वृश्चिकश्छत्रं कुम्भश्छत्रङ्घटस्य च।**

</div>

<div>

**उच्चस्थानमिति ज्ञात्वाऽऽरूढे स्यादुदये यदि।**

</div>

<div>

**मरणं न भवेत्तस्य रोगिणो नात्र संशयः॥२३०॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Aaroodha or Udaya Lagna synchronizes with the Chhatra Raasi, i.e. Scorpio for Scorpio, Leo for Leo, Taurus for Taurus, and Aquarius for Aquarius, and hence declared to be in exaltation, the person concerned about when the enquiry is made will not certainly die.

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


*Note*: In Prasna Saastra, if the same Raasi becomes Chhatra Raasi to itself, it is stated to be in exaltation. 230

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**तुलाया कार्मुकं छत्रं नीचं मृत्युर्विपर्यये।  
मेषस्य मिथुनं छत्रं नीचं मृत्युर्विपर्यये॥२३१॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Libra happens to be Chhatra Raasi for Sagittarius (as either Aaroodha or Udaya) it is stated to be in debilitation, and the person's life will be in danger. One cannot be certain of death here, but if, however, Sagittarius happens to be Chhatra for Libra, death is certain. Likewise, if Gemini is the Chhatra Raasi for Aries, it is debilitated, the person will be in danger, but in the reverse case Aries being Chhatra for Gemini, death is certain. 231

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**कन्या छत्रं कुलीरस्य नीचं मृत्युर्विपर्यये।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नक्रस्य मीनच्छत्रं च नीचं मृत्युर्विपर्यये।  
नीचे न शाम्यति व्याधिर्मृत्यो मरणमादिशेत्॥२३२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Virgo is Chhatra for Cancer, it is in debilitation, and hence the person's life is in danger. But if Cancer is Chhatra Raasi for Virgo, death is certain. If Pisces is Chhatra for Capricom, it is in debilitation and hence life is endangered; but if Capricorn is Chhatra for Pisces, death is certain. The debilitated Raasi indicates danger to life and no cure of disease. But the Mrityudasaa foretells certain death. 232

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ग्रहेषु बलवान्सूर्यो यदि मृत्युस्तदाग्निना।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मन्दः क्षुधा जलेनेन्दुः शीतेन कविरुच्यते॥२३३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If at the time of Prasna, the Sun is strong, death by fire is likely; if Saturn is strong, death by hunger; if the Moon is strong, death by water; and if Venus is strong, death by freezing. 233

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**बुघस्तुषारवाताभ्यां शस्त्रेणारो बली यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**राहुर्विषेण जीवस्तु कुक्षिरोगेण नश्यति॥२३४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 And if Mercury is strong at the time of Prasna, death will take place by snow and storm; if Mars is strong, death by weapons; if Rahu is strong, death by poisoning; and if Jupiter is strong, death by some disease in the stomach is to be predicted. 234

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**विधोः षष्टाष्टमे पापास्सप्तमे वा यदि स्थिताः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**रोगमृत्युस्थलाभ्यां वा रोगिणां मरणं ध्रुवम्॥२३५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आरूढं मरणस्थानं तस्मादष्टमगश्शशी।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पापाः पश्यन्तिचेन्मृत्युं रोगिणां कथयेत्सुधीः॥२३६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 By finding the malefics in the 6th, 8th or 7th from the Moon at the time of Prasna, the nature of death of the diseased person is to be predicted. If, as stated above, the Aaroodha Lagna happens to be the house of death and from there in the 8th place is the Moon aspected by malefics, death to the diceased one is to be told by the wise. 235–236

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तृतीये भानुसंयुक्ते दशमे पापसंयुते।  
दशाहान्मरणं ब्रूयाच्छुक्रजीवौ तृतीयगौ।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सप्ताहान्मरणंब्रूयाद्रोगिणामतिबुद्धिमान्॥२३७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Sun is at the third place from the Udaya Lagna, or a malefic in the 10th place death in 10 days is likely. If Venus or Jupiter is in the 3rd place from Udaya Lagna, death to the diceased person in 7 days is to be predicted. 237

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदये चतुरस्रे वा पापास्त्वष्टदिनान्मृतिः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**लग्नाद्वितीयगाः पापाश्र्चतुर्दशदिनान्मृतिः॥२३८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If malefics are in Udaya Raasi or in the 4th or 8th place, death in 8 days is likely. If malefic is in the 2nd place from Udaya Lagna death in 14 days is likely. 238

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**त्रिदिनान्मरणं किन्तु दशमे पापसंयुते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तस्मात्सप्तमगे पापे दशाहान्मरणं भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**निधनारूढगे पापे दृष्टे वा मरणं भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तत्तद्ग्रहवशेनैव दिनमासादिनिर्णयः॥२३९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If a malefic is in the 10th place, death in 3 days is to be predicted. If a malefic is in the 7th place from Udaya Lagna, death in 10 days is likely. Along with this, one has to reckon the days and months given for various planets and give the prediction accordingly.  
* Note:* Some other text books affirm that if the bouse of death is a fixed sign, death will be in the native country; if it is a moveable sign, death will be in a foreign country; and if it is a common sign, death will be in the neighbouring country. 239

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681983526.png)  
**Chapter XIII**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***ON HEAVENLY ABODE***

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ग्रहोच्चेस्वर्गमायाति रिपौ मृगकुले भवः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नीचे नरकमायाति मित्रे मित्रकुले भवः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्वक्षेत्रे स्वजने जन्म मृतानां कथयेद्बुधः॥२४०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If at the time of Prasna, the Udaya Lagna is in exaltation, the dead man will attain the heavenly abode. If it is in an inimical sign the dead man will be reborn as an animal. If it is in debilitation he will go to hell. If it is a friendly house he will be reborn in a friend's house. If it is in its own house he will be reborn among his family or relatives. 240

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681983526.png)  
**Chapter XIV**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***ON****FOOD***  


</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कथयामि विशेषेण भुक्तद्रव्यस्य निर्णयम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पाकभाण्डानि भुक्तानि व्यञ्जनानि रसास्ततः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सह भौक्तन्भाजनानि तद्दातृस्नेहिनो रिपून्॥२४१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 I will now tell you about the kind of food eaten–about the vessels in which the meal was prepared, the articles of food like vegetables, pulses, etc., their tastes, the guestswith whom the meal was taken, the plates on which food was served, the friends of the host and his enemies too – all in detail. 241

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मेषराशौ भवेच्छागं वृषभे गव्यमुच्यते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**धनुर्मिथुनसिह्मेषु मत्स्यमांसादिभोजनम्॥२४२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If at the time of Prasna, Aries is rising, the food taken is mutton; if Taurus, it is beef, is Gemini, Leo or Sagittarius is rising, it is fish. 242

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नक्रालिकर्कमीनेषु परिपक्वफलादिकम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तुलाकन्याघटेष्वेव शुद्धान्नमिति कीर्तयेत्॥२४३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If it is Cancer, Capricorn, Scorpio or Pisces, the food eaten is ripe fruit; and if it is Virgo, Libra or Aquarius, the meal is good rice. 243

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**भानौ, तिक्तकदुक्षारमिश्रं भोजनमुच्यते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कृष्णान्नं क्षौद्रसंयुक्तं भूमिपुत्रस्य भोजनम्॥ २४४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If at the time of Prasna the Sun is rising, the food has salty, hot and bitter taste; if it is Mars rising, the food is mixed with honey and black in colour. 244

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**भर्जितान्युपदंशानि सौम्यस्याहुर्मनीषिणः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पायसान्नं घृतयुतं गुरोर्भोजनमीरितम्॥२४५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


If it is Mercury rising, the food is well–spiced and servedwith pickles. 245

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**सतैलकोद्रवान्न च भवेन्मन्दस्य भोजनम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चणकं राहुकेत्वोश्च रसवर्ग उहाहृतः॥२४६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


If it is Jupiter the food is served with ghee and sweets; if it is Saturn, the food is rye mixed oil; and if it is either Rahu or Ketu, the food is made of some grams. 246

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**जीवस्य मषवटकं सूपमिश्रं तु भोजनम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चन्द्रस्य कन्दप्रसवमत्स्याद्यैर्भोजनं भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**क्षौद्रापूपपयोयुग्भिव्यंजनैर्भोजनं भृगोः॥२४७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 From Jupiter rising one can predict cutlets (or vada) and dhall–mixed rice; from the Moon to be predicted tubers, flowers and fish; from Venus rising is to be understood that the food consists of sweet, milk–products etc. 247

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ओजराशौ शुभैर्दृष्टे सुरुच्या भोजनं भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**समराशौ मन्दरुच्या भुंक्तेऽल्पं पापवीक्षिते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**केचित्पश्यन्ति पापाश्चेत्पुराणान्नं क्षुघार्दितः॥२४८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If an odd sign is rising and aspected by benefics the food is tasty and refreshing; and if it is a common sign aspected by malefics, the food will be moderate and little. But some predict that if a common sign is aspected by amalefic, the food will be old and rotten and; taken on ahungry stomach. 248

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अर्कारौ मांसभोक्तारावुशनश्चन्द्रभोगिनः।  
नवनीतघृतक्षीरदधिभिर्भोजनं भवेत्॥२४९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Non–vegetarian food is predicted by the Sun and Marsrising; food with butter, milk, curd and ghee if it is Venus, the Moon or Rahu rising. 249

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जलराशिषु पापेषु ससौम्येष्वीक्षितेषु च।  
सतैलभोजनं ब्रूयादितिज्ञात्वा विचक्षणः॥२५०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**पूर्वोक्तधातुवर्गेण थाजनानि विनिर्दिशेत्।  
मूलवर्गेण शाकादिनुपदंशान्वदेद्बुधः॥२५१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**जीववर्गेण भोक्तंश्च मत्स्यमाषादिकानपि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सर्वमालोक्य निश्चित्य प्रश्नान्नृणां वुघो वदेत्॥२५२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If a malefic is posited in a watery sign and (even if) associated with a benefic or aspected by it, articles of food fried in oil are to be predicted. A wise man by reckoning the nature of signs and planets with regard to food articles (mentioned in verses 243–247), should predict appropriately by noting the rising sign and planet at the time of Prasna. All considerations have to be taken into account before giving a prediction. 250–252

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681983526.png)  
**Chapter XV**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***ON DREAMS***

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div>

**स्वप्ने यान् परिपश्यन्ति सर्वान्वक्ष्यामि सर्वथा।**

</div>

<div>

**मेषोदये देवगृहं प्रासादाः संभवन्ति च।**

</div>

<div>

**वृषोदये दिनाधीशे ज्ञातगेहस्य दर्शनम्॥२५३॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Whatever things and events are seen in dreams shall now be narrated. If the Udaya Raasi is Aries, one will dream of temples and storeyed houses. If the Raasi is Taurus but aspected by the Sun, the same kind of dream can be predicted. 253

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**वृश्चिकस्योदयेऽर्कारौ व्याकुलं मृतदर्शनम्।**

</div>

<div>

**मिथुनस्योदये विप्रं तपस्विवचनानि च॥२५४॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If at the time of Prasna, Scorpio is rising, with the Sun and Mars posited therein, the dream will be full of sadness, and he may dream about a dead man too. If Gemini is rising, he will dream of brahmins and ascetics teaching scriptures. 254

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**कुलीरस्योदये क्षेत्रे सस्यं दृष्ट्वा पुनर्गृहम्।**

</div>

<div>

**तृणान्यादाय हस्ताभ्यां गच्छतीति विनिर्दिशेत्॥२५५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Cancer is rising he will dream of going to the fields and coming back home with grass in his hands. 255

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**सिह्मोदये किरातांश्च महिषान् गिरिपद्धतिम्।**

</div>

<div>

**कन्योदयेपि चारूढे मुण्डस्त्रीभ्यः पिबन्त्यपः॥२५६॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Leo is rising, he will dream of hunters of mountains and buffaloes. If Virgo is either Aaroodha or Udaya Lagna, he will dream of drinking water given by a nude woman. 256

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**तुलोदये नृपं स्वर्णं वणिजं च स पश्यति।**

</div>

<div>

**वृश्चिकस्योदये स्वप्ने पश्यत्यलिमृगादिकम्।**

</div>

<div>

**वृषांश्चैव तथा दृष्टा स्वप्ने ब्रूयादशङ्कितः॥२५७॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If it is Libra rising, he will see kings, gold and merchants in his dream. If it is Scorpio, he will dream of bees and beasts. He will see bulls but won't be frightened; he will drive them away. 257

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**उदये धनुषः पश्येत्पुष्पं पक्वफलं लभेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**मृगोदये नदीं नारीं पुमान्स्वप्नेषु पश्यति।  
कुम्भोदये च मुकुरं मीने स्वर्णं जलाशयम्॥२५८॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If it is Sagittarius, he will dream of flowers. He will get ripe fruits in his dream. If it is Capricorn ‘rising, he will see rivers and girls in the dream. If it is Aquarius, he will dreamof mirrors; if Pisces, he will dream of gold, lakes and tanks. 258

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**तुर्ये तिष्ठति शुक्रे च राजतं वस्तु पश्यति।**

</div>

<div>

**आदिस्यश्चेन्मृतान् पुंसः पतनं शुष्कशाखिनाम्।**

</div>

<div>

**चन्द्रश्चेत्प्लवनं सिन्धौ राहुर्मद्यं विषं भवेत्॥२५९॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Venus is in the 4th house from Udaya Raasi, he will dream of seeing silver vessels. If the Sun is in the 4th, he will dream of dead men and of falling from barren trees. If the Moon is in the 4th, he will dream of swimming in the sea; and if it is Rahu, he will dream of wine and poison. 259

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**अत्र किञ्चिद्विशेषोऽस्ति च्छत्रारूढोदयेषु च।**

</div>

<div>

**शुक्रस्थितश्चेत्सुश्वेतसौघं सौम्यो ऽमरान्वदेत्॥२६०॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 But there is a special point to be noticed; if Venus is in Chhatra, Aaroodha or Udaya Raasi, he will dream of white mansions; and if Mercury, he will dream of gods. 260

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**चतुर्थस्थ वशात्स्वप्नं ब्रूयाद्ग्रहनिरीक्षणैः।**

</div>

<div>

**अत्रानुक्तं तदखिलं ब्रूयात्पूर्वोक्तवर्त्मना॥२६१॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

Dreams are to be interpreted in terms of the planets inthe 4th house from Udaya Raasi and in terms of planets aspecting the 4th house. 261

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681879171.png)

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

**Chapter XVI**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***OMENS***

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div>


**अथोभयर्क्षे पथिको दुर्निमित्तो निवर्तते।**

</div>

<div>

**चरोदये निमित्तानि त्वादायेयादितीरयेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**स्थिरोदये निमित्तानां विरोधे न च गच्छति॥२६२॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

When giving predictions about travel, one must note that if a common sign is rising at the time of Prasna, the pilgrim will return home because of bad omens. If a moving sign is rising he will not travel due to bad omens. 262

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**चन्द्रोदये दिवाभीतचाषपारावतादयः।  
शकुना भयदा दृष्टा इति ब्रूयाद्विचक्षणः॥२६३॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is rising in Udaya Lagna, bad omens byowls, partidges and pigeons are predicted. 263

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**गुरूदये तथाकाकभारद्वाजादिपक्षिणः।  
मन्दोदये कुलिङ्गस्स्याज्ज्ञोदये पिङ्गलो भवेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**सूर्योदये च गरुडः सव्यासव्यवशाद्भवेत्॥२६४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Jupiter is rising, the pilgrim will see crows and long–tailed sparrows. If Saturn is rising, he will see a special typeof bird called ‘Kulinga' and if Mercury, he will see a bird called 'Pingala'. If the Sun is on the right side of Udaya Raasi, he will see the eagle flying on his right side; and if the Sun is on the left side the eagle also will be seen on the left side. 264

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**स्थिरराशा स्थिरान्पश्येध्वरे तिर्यग्गतानिति।**

</div>

<div>

**उभयेऽध्वनि वृत्तिस्स्याद्ग्रहस्थितिवशादमी॥२६५॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

If a fixed sign is rising at the time of Prasna, he will see definite good omens while starting; if a moving sign, he will see birds flying cross–wise; and if a common sign is rising, he will see omens on the way. 265  

**राहोर्गोघा विधोश्चाषो ज्ञस्य छुच्छुन्दरीभवेत्।  
दधि शुक्रस्य जीवस्य क्षीरं सर्पिरुदाहृतम्॥२६६॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 What omens will be seen when planets are in the Udaya Lagna? If it is Rahu in the Udaya Lagna, he will see the Iguana; if the Moon, he will see partridges; if it is Mercury, he will see a land–rat; if it is Venus, he will see a milkmaid bringing curd and if it is Jupiter he will see milk and ghee. 266  

**भानोश्च श्वेतगरुडः शिवा भौमस्य कीर्तिता।  
शनेस्तस्करवह्नीच निमित्तं दृष्टमादिशेत्॥२६७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If it is the Sun, he will see a white eagle; if Mars, a fox; if Saturn, fire and thief, these are the omens to be predicted. 267

</div>

<div>


**भौमस्य श्वानभल्लूकभारद्वाजशशा इति।**

</div>

<div>

**उलृकस्तित्तिरिश्चैव कपोतश्च गुरोरमी॥२६८॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If it is Mars in the Udaya Lagna, he will see dog, bear and hare;, if it is Venus, he will see flying birds and chameleon. 268

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681880096.png)  
**Chapter XVII**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***ON MARRIAGES***

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div>

**शुक्रस्य पक्षिणो ब्रूयाद्गगने सरटस्तथा।**

</div>

<div>

**जीवकाण्डप्रकारेण पक्षिणो न्यान्विचारयेत्॥२६९॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**प्रश्नं वैवाहिके लग्ने कुजसूर्यबुघा यदि।  
वैधव्यं शीघ्रमायाति सा नारी नात्र संशयः॥२७०॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 At the time of Prasna regarding marriage, if the Sun, Mars and Mercury are in Udaya Lagna, marriage will be celebrated soon, but the girl will be widowed shortly. 269–270  

**उदये मन्दगे नारी रिक्ता मृतसुता भवेत्।  
चन्द्रोदयेतु मरणं दंपत्योश्शीघ्रमेव च।  
सितजीवबुधा लग्ने यदि तौ दीर्घजीविनौ॥२७१॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Saturn is in the Prasna Lagna, the girl to be married will be poor and she will have children who will soon die. If the Moon is in the Prasna Lagna, the couple will shortly meet with death.  
 But if Venus, Jupiter and Mercury are in Prasna Lagna, the couple will live long happily. 271

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**द्वितीयस्थे निशानाथे बहुपुत्रवती भवेत्।  
स्थिता यद्यर्कमन्दारा मनः क्लेशो दरिद्रता॥२७२॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is in the 2nd place from Prasna Lagna, the girl to be married will give birth to; many children. If the Sun, Saturn or Mars is in the 2nd place, the couple will be sorrowful and suffer from poverty. 272

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**द्वितीये राहुसंयुक्ते सा भार्या व्यभिचारिणी।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुभग्रहाः द्वितीयस्था माङ्गल्यबहुपुत्रदाः॥२७३॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Rahu is in the 2nd place, the wife will be unchaste. If benefic planets are in the 2n place she will live long with her husband, blessed with children. 273

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**तृतीये जीवराहू चेत्सा वन्ध्या भवति ध्रुवम्।**

</div>

<div>

**अन्ये तृतीयराशिस्था धनसौभाग्यवृद्धिदाः॥२७४॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Jupiter or Rahu is in the 3rd place from the Prasna Lagna the wife will remain barren. But if other planets are in the 3rd place she will be happy, prosperous and blessed. 274

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**चतुर्थेऽर्कनिशाधीशौ तिष्ठतो यदि पापिनौ।**

</div>

<div>

**शनौ स्तन्येन हीना स्यादहो सापत्न्यवत्यसौ।**

</div>

<div>

**बुध शुक्रारजीवाश्वेदल्प जीवनवत्यसौ॥२७५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If malefics like the Sun and the Moon are in the 4th place, or even if Saturn occupies it, the wife will have no breast milk to feed the babies. If Rahu is in the 4th place, her husband will have a concubine. If Mercury, Venus, Mars or Jupiter is in the 4th place she will be short–lived. 275

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**पञ्चमे यदि सौरिस्स्याद्वयाधियाधिना सा प्रपीडिता।**

</div>

<div>

**शुक्रजीवबुधास्स्युश्चेब्दहुपुत्रवती वधूः॥२७६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Saturn is, in the 5th place from Prasna Lagna, the girl to be married will suffer from illness; if Venus, Jupiter or Mercury is in the 5th place, she will have many children. 276

</div>

<div>


**चन्द्रादित्यौ तु वन्ध्या स्यादहिश्चेन्मरणं भवेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**आरश्चेत्पुत्रनाशस्स्यात्प्रश्ने पाणिग्रहोचिते॥२७७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Sun or the Moon is in the 5th place, the woman will be barren. If Rahu is in the 5th place, her son will die. If Mars is in the 5th place the woman will be barren. If Mars is in the 5th place, destruction of her son can be predicted. 277

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**षष्ठे शशीचेद्विधवा बुधः कलहकारिणी।**

</div>

<div>

**षष्ठेतिष्ठति शुक्रे च दीर्घमङ्गलहारिणी।  
अन्ये तिष्ठन्ति चेन्नारी सुखिनी वृद्धिमत्यपि॥२७८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Moon is in the 6th place from Prasna Lagna, the girl to be a married will soon be a widow. If Mercury is in the6th place, the married girl creates conflict in the house. If venus in the 6th house, she will live long happily with her husband. Any planet other than the Moon, Mercury and Venus in the 6th house will confer increased happiness and prosperity to the girl to be married. 278

</div>

<div>


**सप्तमस्थे शनौ नारी तरसा विधवा भवेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**व्याधिग्रस्ता भवेन्नारी सप्तमस्थे रवौ यदि॥२७९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The girl will soon be widowed, if Saturn is in the 7th place from Prasna Lagna. The Sun in the 7th place will make the girl suffer from illness. 279

</div>

<div>


**सप्तमस्थे निशानाथे ज्वरपीडावती भवेत्।  
परेणापहृता याति कुजे तिष्ठति सप्तमे॥२८०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The Moon in the 7th place from Prasna Lagna will also afflict the married girl with fever. If Mars is in the 7th place, she will be taken away by another man. 280

</div>

<div>


**बुधजीवौ समृद्धिस्याद्राहुश्चेद्विधवा भवेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**शुक्रश्चेत्सप्तमे राशौ वधूर्मृत्युं प्रयास्यति॥२८१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 Prosperity will come to the girl to be married, if Jupiter or Mercury is in the 7th place. If Rahu is in the 7th place, she will be widowed. She will die soon after marriage if Venus is in the 7th place from the Prasna Lagna. 281

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**अष्टमस्था शुऋगुरुभुजङ्गा नाशयन्ति च।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शनि ज्ञौवृद्धिदौ चन्द्रो मारयत्येव भामिनीम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आदित्यारौ पुनर्भूस्स्यात्प्रने वैवाहिके वधोः॥२८२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 Venus, Jupiter and Rahu, if they happen to occupy the 8th place from Prasna Lagna, will cause destruction. But Saturn and Mercury in the 8th will confer increased benefit to the girl to be married. The Moon too in the 8th will cause destruction. The Sun or Mars in the 8th will make the girl get married twice.  
 Note: Being betrothed to one, the wedding may not come through, and she will marry another. 282

</div>

<div>


**नवमे यदि सौम्यस्स्याद्व्याधिहीना भवेद्वधूः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जीवचन्द्रौ यदि स्यातां वहुपुत्रवती भवेत्।  
अन्ये तिष्ठन्ति नवमे यदिवन्ध्या नसंशयः॥२८३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 Mercury in the 9th place from Prasna Lagna will rid the would be married girl of all illness. Jupiter or the Moon is in the 9th place, she will get many children. If other planets are there in the 9th place (i.e. the Sun, Mars, Venus, Saturn, Rahu or Ketu) the girl to be married will remain barren. 283

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**दशमे यदि चन्द्रस्स्याद्वन्ध्या भवति भामिनी।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**भार्गवो यदि वेश्यास्याद्विधवाकिंकुजादयः।  
रिक्ता गुरु ज्ज्ञादित्यौ यदि तस्याश्शुभंवदेत्॥२८४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Moon is in the 10th place from Prasna Lagna, the girl will also remain barren. If Venus is in the 10th she will be unchaste. If Mars or Saturn is in the 10th, she will become a widow. If Jupiter is in 10th, she will be poor, but if Mercury, or the Sun is in the 10th she will be happy and prosperous. 284

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**लाभस्थानगतास्सर्वे पुत्रसौभाग्यवृद्धिदाः।**

</div>

<div>

**लग्नाद्वादशगश्चन्द्रो यदि स्यान्नाशमादिशेत्।**

</div>

<div>

**शनिभौमौ यदि स्यातां सुरापानवती भवेत्॥२८५॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 All planets in the house of gain (i.e. the 11th place from Prasna Lagna, will confer wealth, children and happiness to the girl to be married. But if the Moon is in the 12th house, unhappiness and destruction are to be predicted. Saturn and Mars in the 12th place or aspecting it will make her a drunkard. 285

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div>

**बुधे पुत्रवती जीवे धनधान्यवती वधूः।**

</div>

<div>

**सर्पादित्यौ स्थितौ वन्ध्या शुक्रे सुखवती भवेत्॥२८६॥**

</div>

<div>



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Mercury is in the 12th place, the girl will have male issues; and if Jupiter is in the 12th, she will have wealth and grains in plenty Rahu or Sun in the 12th will make her barren; but Venus in the 12th will make her happy and prosperous. 286

</div>

![](../books_images/1681884136.png)

<div style="text-align:center">

**Chapter XVIII**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***ON LOVE AND CONJUGAL FELICITY***

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**सीपुंसोरतिभोगांश्च स्नेहास्नेहौ पतिव्रतम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुद्धाशुद्धौ क्रमात्प्रोक्ताश्शास्त्रे ज्ञानप्रदीपके॥२८७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 This science (Gnaana Pradeepikaa) teaches also about the relationship between husband and wife, conjugal happiness, chastity, and of impurity too. 287

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पृच्छकादुदयारूढकेन्द्रेषु भुजगो यदि।  
तेषां दुष्टास्स्त्रियस्साक्षाद्देवानामप्यसंशयः॥२८८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Rahu is posited in trines of Aarpodha or Udaya Lagna at the time of Prasna, the wives of the enquirers would be quarrelsome women, undoubtedly. 288

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**लग्नादेकादशेऽस्ते च तृतीये दशमे शशी।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जीवदृष्टियुतस्तिष्ठेद्यदि भार्या पतिव्रता॥२८९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Moon is posited in the 11th, 7th, 3rd or 10th from Lagna and aspected by Jupiter the wife would be chaste. 289

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**चन्द्रं पश्यन्ति पुंखेटास्तेन युक्ता भवन्ति चेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तद्भार्या दुर्जनीभूयादितिशास्त्रविदो विदुः॥२९०।।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If male planets are either associated with or aspecting the Moon, the person's wife wil be unchaste. 290

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सप्तमस्थद्विषत्खेटेर्दृष्टो नीचारिगश्शशी।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**बन्धुविद्वेषिणी लोके भ्रष्टा स्याच्च शुभे शुभा॥२९१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The Moon debilitated or posited in an inimical house, if aspected by malefic planets in the 7th house, indicates that the person's wife would be abusing his relations, and would stray away from social conventions. But if the Moon is associated with or aspected by benefic planets, she would be of good character. 291

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**भानुजीवौ निशाधीशं पश्यन्तौ वा युतौ यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पतिव्रता भवेन्नारी रूपिणीति वदेद्बुधः॥२९२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Sun or Jupiter is associated with or aspecting the Moon, the wife would be beautful and chaste. 292

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुक्रेण युक्तो दृष्टो वा भोमश्चेत्परगामिनी।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**बृहस्पतिर्बुधाराभ्यां युक्तश्चेत्कन्यकारतिः॥२९३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

If Mars is associated with or aspected by Venus, the wife would have liaison with other persons. If Mars is associated with Jupiter and Mercury, there would be union with a virgin. 293

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**शुकवर्गयुते भौमे भौमवर्गयुते भृगौ।  
प्रष्टुस्स्याद्विधवा भार्या तस्या दोषो भविष्यति॥२९४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Mars is in the Varga of Venus or Venus in the Varga of Mars at the time of Prasna, the person's wife will become a widow. She will also be corrupt. 294  

**भानुवर्गयुते शुक्रे राजस्त्रीरतिभागिनी।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जीववर्गयुते चन्द्रे स्नेहेन रतिभागिनी॥२९५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 At the time of Prasna, if Venus gets the Varga (strength) of the Sun, the wife will have the happiness and prosperity of a royal princess. If the Moon gets the Varga of Jupiter, she will have conjugal bliss in a happy way. 295

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**चन्द्रः स्त्रीवर्गयुक्तश्चेत् स्त्री स्वतन्त्रवती भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शनैश्चरेण युक्तश्चेदतीव व्यभिचारिणी॥२९६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 At the time of Prasna if Venus gets the Varga (strength) of a female planet, the wife will be 'liberated'. And if the Moon is associated with Saturn, she will be a prostitute. 296

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**पापवर्गयुते दृष्टे शुक्रे चेद्व्यभिचारिणी।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अरिवर्गयुतश्चन्द्रो यद्यमित्रवधूरतिः॥२९७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Venus gets the Varga (strength) of a malefic or is aspected by it, the woman will be unchaste. If the Moon getsthe Varga of a malefic or aspected by it, there may be union with an enemy's wife (or woman in the enemy's camp). 297

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**नीचवर्गयुतश्चन्द्रो नीचस्त्रीभोगकामुकः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मित्रवर्गयुतश्चन्द्रो मित्रवर्गवधूरतिः॥२९८॥**

</div>
