<div style="text-align:justify">


 If at the time of Prasna the Moon has 'Neecha Varga', the person will have desire for union with a low woman. If the Moon is in association with a friendly class of planets he will have union with a friendly kind of woman. 298

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**स्वक्षेत्रे यदि शीतांशुस्स्वभार्यायां रतिर्भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्ववर्गयुक्तश्चन्द्रश्चेत्स्वोच्च्ववंशस्त्रिया रतिः॥२९९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is in its own house at the time of Prasna, the person will have conjugal enjoyment with his wife. If the Moon gets its own Varga (strength) the person will have union with a woman higher than his own class. 299

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदासीनग्रहयुतो दृष्टो वा यदि चन्द्रमाः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदासीनक्धूभोग इतिचाहुर्मनीषिणः॥३००॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is associated with an equal planet or aspected by it, the person will have union with a reckless woman. 300

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**लग्ने च दशमेऽस्ते च पञ्चमे शनियुक् शशी।  
चोररूपेण कथयेद्रात्रौ स्वप्नवधूरतिम्॥३०१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Moon is associated with Saturn in the 1st, 10th, 7th or 5th place, the person will in the night have union with a sleeping woman who has a thief's appearance. 301

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**ओजोदये तदधिपे त्वेकमैथुनमुच्यते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**समोदये तदधिपे समस्थे द्वे रती तथा॥३०२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 At the time of Prasna, if the rising sign is an odd one and its lord too is in an odd sign the person will have sex relationship once. But if the rising sign is an even one and its lord too is in an even sign, the enjoyment will be on two occasions. 302

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**लग्नेश्वरबलं ज्ञात्वा तेषां किरणसङ्ख्यया।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अथवा कथयेद्विद्वांत्सन्द्रष्टृग्रहसङ्ख्यया॥३०३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 By determining the strength of the rising planet and counting its rays or the rays of the planets aspecting it, the number of times of sex relationship is to be predicted. 303

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चन्द्रे भौमयुते दृष्टे कलहेन पृथक्शयः**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**भृगौ सौरियुते दृष्टे स्वस्त्रीकलह उच्यते॥३०४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon, is associated with Mars or aspected by it, sleeping in separate beds by the couple due to quarrel is to be predicted. If Venus is associated with Saturn or aspected by it, there will be quarrel between the couple. 304

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**चतुर्थे च तृतीये च पञ्चमे सप्तमेपि वा।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चन्द्रे शुक्रयुते दृष्टे स्वस्त्रिया कलहो भवेत्॥ ३०५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 The couple's misunderstanding and strife is predicted also when the Moon is associated with or aspected by Venus, in any one of the places: the 4th, 3rd, 5th or 7th from the Udaya Lagna. 305  

**तदीयवसनच्छेदं रचितं परिकीर्तयेत्।  
सप्तमे पापसंयुक्ते दशमे पापसंयुते॥३०६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If there is any relationship with a malefic in the 7th or 10th house, the woman's sari would be torn. 306  

**तृतीये बुघसंयुक्ते स्त्रीविवादात्स्थले शयः।  
लग्ने चन्द्रयुते भौमे द्वितीयस्थे तदा निशि॥३०७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Mercury is in the 3rd house the person will lie down on the floor due to quarrel with his wife. If at the time of Prasna the Moon is in the Udaya Lagna and Mars in the 2nd house, the same condition will prevail in the night asstated above. 307

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जागरं चोरभीत्यर्थे राशिनक्षत्रसंधिषु।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**दृष्टश्चेद्विधवाभोगमकरोदिति कीर्तयेत्॥३०८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Prasna is made at the time of the junction of signs or the junction of stars, lying awake without sleep due to fearof thieves is to be predicted. If the above is aspected by other planets, union with widow is possible. 308

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तस्संघौ शुक्रसौम्यौ चेत्तदा दास्याः पति वदेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**यत्र कुत्रापि शशिनं पापाः पश्यन्ति चेत्तदा।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पुंसि चासज्जयति वधूः शुभाश्चेत्पुरुषप्रिया॥३०९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If during the junction of sign or star is posited Venus or Mercury, at the time of Prasna, union with a prostitute can be predicted.. If at Prasna time, malefics are aspecting the Moon, wherever it may be situated, prediction can be made that the wife is loving another person. But if benefics are aspecting the Moon, the wife will be friendly and loving to the husband. 309

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सात्विकाश्चन्द्रजीवार्का राजसौ शुक्रसोमजौ।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तामसौ शनिभूपुत्रौ चैव स्त्रीपुंगुणास्मृताः॥३१०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 The Moon, the Sun and Jupiter are of a saattvik nature; Venus and Mercury are of a raajasik nature; Saturn and Mars are of a taamasik nature.

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 From the nature of the planets are to be determined the character and habits of men and women. 310

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681906352.png)

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

**Chapter XIX**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***OF CHILDREN***

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**पुत्रोत्पत्तिनिमित्तं यत्प्रश्ने स्त्रीभिः कृते सति।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदेयारूढछत्रेषु राहुश्चेद्गर्भमादिशेत्॥३११॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 As women ask about the birth of children to them I shall narrate the planetary conditions precedent for them. If Rahu is in Udaya Lagna, Aaroodha Lagna, or in the Moon's Lagna, conception will take place. 311

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**लग्नाद्वा चन्द्रलग्नाद्वा त्रिकोणे सप्तमेऽपि वा।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**बृहस्पतौ स्थिते वापि यदि पश्यति गर्भिणी॥ ३१२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 At the time of Prasna, if Jupiter is in the 5th, 9th or 7th place from Udaya Lagna or the Moon's sign, or if Jupiter aspects those houses, conception can be predicted. 312

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**शुभवर्गेण युक्तश्चेत्सुखप्रसवमादिशेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अरिनीचगृहस्थश्चेत्सुतारिष्टं भविष्यति॥३१३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Jupiter gets the influence of benefics, parturition (confinement) of the child will be easy; if Jupiter is in debilitation or inimical sign, misfortune (death) to the child is to be predicted. 313

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**प्रश्नकाले तु परिघौ वृषे गर्भवती भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तदन्तस्थग्रहवशात्पुंस्त्रीभेदं वदेद्बुधः।  
यत्रतत्र स्थितश्चन्द्रः शुभैर्युक्तस्तु गर्भिणी॥ ३१४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If at the time of Prasna the Upagraha Parivesha is in Taurus, the woman will be pregnant. From the planets associated with Parivesha, the sex of the child in the embryo can be determined. If at the time of Prasna, the Moon in whatever sign, is associated with a benefic, conception will take place. 314

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**लग्नात्त्रिनवभूतेषु शुक्रादित्येन्दवः क्रमात्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तिष्ठन्ति चेन्न गर्भस्स्यादेकत्रैते स्थिता नच॥३१५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If in the 3rd, 9th and 5th places respectively Venus, the Sun, and the Moon are posited, or if the three planets are together in any one of the three places, conception will not take place. 315

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

*Sex Determination:*  
 I will now describe the means by which the sex of the child in the embryo can be determined.

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्त्रीपुंविवेके गर्भिण्याः पृष्टे वा तत्र कालके।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**परिवेषादिकैर्दृष्टे तस्या गर्भो विनश्यति॥३१६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 At the time of Prasna, if the Upagraha Parivesha aspectsthe Lagna there will be abortion. 316

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**लग्नादोजस्थिते चन्द्रे पुत्रं सृते समे सुताम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**वशान्नक्षत्रराशीनां यथायोगं सुतं सुताम्॥३१७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is at an odd sign from the Prasna Lagna, the child will be male. But the Moon is at an even sign from the Prasna Lagna, the child will be female. From the star and sign at the time of Prasna, the sex of the child also can be predicted. 317

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**लग्नात्तृनीयनवमदशमैकादशेष्वपि।  
भानुः स्थितश्चेत्पुत्रस्स्यात्तथैव च शनैश्चरः॥३१८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Sun or Saturn is in the 3rd, 9th, 10th or 11th place from Prasna Lagna, a male child will be born. 318  


</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ओजस्थानगतास्सर्वे ग्रहाश्चेत्पुत्रसंभवः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**समस्थानगतास्सर्वे यदि पुत्री न संशयः॥३१९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If, at the time of Prasna, all the planets are in an odd sign, amale will be born. If all planets are in a neutral sign, a female child will be born. 319

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आरूढात्सप्तमं राशिं यावच्छीतांशुरेष्यति।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तावन्नक्षत्रसंख्याकैस्सृते सा दिवसैस्सुतम्॥ ३२०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 The time taken for the Moon to transit from the Aaroodha Raasi to its 7th place or the number of stars in the signs from Aaroodha to the 7th place will give the number of days by which the woman will deliver the child. 320

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681983526.png)  
**Chapter XX**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***OF MISFORTUNES***

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**सुतारिष्टमथो वक्ष्ये सद्यः प्रत्ययकारकम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**लग्नात्वष्ठस्थिते चन्द्रे तदस्ते पापसंयुते॥३२१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**मातुस्सुतस्य मरणं किन्तु पंचमषष्ठयोः**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पापास्तिष्ठन्ति चेन्मातुर्मरणं भवति ध्रुवम्॥३२२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 Now I will describe the misfortunes that are likely to overtake a child. If the Moon is in the 6th place from Prasna Lagna, and if a malefic is posited in the 7th place from the Moon both the mother and the child will die. But if a malefic is there in the 5th or 6th place from the Moon, only the mother will die. 321–322

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**द्वादशे चन्द्रसंयुक्ते पुत्रवामाक्षिनाशनम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**व्ययस्थे भास्करे नशयेत्पुत्रदक्षिणलोचनम्॥३२३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 At the time of Prasna if the Moon is in the 12th place, the baby's left eye, and if the Sun is in the 12th place, the baby's right eye will be blind. 323

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पापाः पश्यन्ति भानुं चेत्पितुर्मरणमादिशेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चन्द्रेण युक्ते दृष्टे वा मातुर्मरणमादिशेत्॥३२४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If malefics aspect the Sun, the father's death, and if the Sun. and the Moon are associated with or aspecting each other, the mother's death is to be predicted. 324

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**चन्द्रादित्यौ गुरुः पश्येन्मातापित्रोर्गदो भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**यदि लग्नगतो राहुर्जीवदृष्टिविवर्जितः॥३२५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**जातस्य मरणं शीघ्रं वदेदत्र न संशयः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**द्वादशस्थावर्कचन्द्रौ नेत्रयुग्मं विनश्यति॥३२६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If at the time of Prasna Jupiter aspects the Sun and the Moon, both the parents will suffer from illness. If Rahu is posited in the Lagna and is aspected by Jupiter, the death of the baby is to be predicted. If the Sun and the Moon are in the 12th place, from the Prasna Lagna, both the eyes of the child will be blind. 325–326

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**षष्ठे वा पंचमे पापाः पश्यन्तीन्दुदिवाकरौ।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मातापित्रोस्तु मरणं तयोर्मन्दः स्थितो यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**भ्रातृनाशं तथा भौमो मातुलस्य मृतिर्वदेत्॥३२७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Sun and the Moon posited in the 6th or 5th place are aspected by malefics, death of the parents is certain. If Saturn is in the 6th or 5th place, death of the brother, and if Mars is there in either of those places, death of the uncle is to be predfcted. 327

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदयादित्रिकानां तु कण्टकेषु शुभा यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मित्रस्वात्युच्चवर्गेषु सर्वारिष्टं विनश्यति॥३२८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If benefics are in the Kendras of Udaya, Aaroodha or Chhatra Lagnas or if benefics are in friendly, own or very exalted, or exalted Vargas all kinds of disaster or accidents will be prevented. 328  

**लग्नं च चन्द्रलग्नं च जीवो यदि न पश्यति।  
पापाः पश्यन्ति चेत्पुत्रो व्यभिचारेण जायते॥३२९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Jupiter does not aspect the Prasna Lagna or the Moon, but only malefics are aspecting; the two Lagnas, the child is born to a different father. 329

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681906691.png)  
**Chapter XXI**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***OF KNIVES***

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**छुरिकालक्षणं सम्यत्मवक्ष्यामि यथातथम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**राहुणा संयुते चन्द्रे शस्त्रभङ्गो भविष्यति॥३३०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 I am now going to tell you all about the ownership and fate of knives. If the Moon is associated with Rahu, the knife will break. If planets in debilitated or enemy's signs aspecting the Moon, the knife will also break. 330

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**नीचारिस्थाः प्रपश्यन्ति यदि शस्त्रस्य भञ्जनम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुभग्रहयुते चन्द्रे दृष्टे वास्ते शुभं भवेत्॥३३१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 But if the Moon is associated with or aspected by benefics and is posited in the 7th place all good will come to the knife. 331

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पापग्रहसमेतेषु छत्रारूढोदयेषु च।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**प्रष्टाप्रश्नाश्रितः किन्तु तदस्त्रेण हतो भवेत्॥३३२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अथवा कलहात्खड्गं परेणापहृतं भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तेषु स्थानेषु सौम्येषु खड्गस्तु शुभदो भवेत्॥३३३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If at the time of Prasna, the Aaroodha, Udaya and Chhatra signs are associated with malefics, the person will be killed by the same knife; or the knife will be taken away by an enemy during a quarrel. But if in the above places benefics are posited, all good will come of the knife. 332–333

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**प्रदर्शितस्य खड्गस्य लग्नेऽस्ते पापसंयुते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**खड्गस्यादौ व्रणं ब्रूयात्त्रिकोणे पापसंयुते॥३३४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शस्त्रभङ्गस्ततो व्योम्नि चतुर्थे पापसंयुते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**खड्गस्य भङ्गो मध्ये स्यादितिज्ञात्वा वदेत्सुधीः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**एकादशे तृतीये च पापे शस्त्राग्रभञ्जनम्॥३३५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 At the time the knife is shown to the astrologist (this is called the Khadga Lagna) if a malefic is posited in the 7th place from that Lagna, the knife will be broken at its lower portion. If malefics are in the 5th or 9th place, the whole knife will be broken at its lower portion. If malefics are in the 10th and 4th, places, the middle portion of the knife will be broken. If in the 11th or 3rd place, the pointed edge of the knife will be broken. 334–335  


</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मित्रस्वात्युच्चनीचारिवर्गानधिगता ग्रहाः।  
तत्तद्वर्गस्थलायत्तं शस्त्रमित्यमिधीयते॥३३६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If plancts in a friendly house aspect the Udaya, Aaroodha or Chhatra Raasis, the knife belongs to a friend; if planets in their own houses aspect the above Raasis the knife belongs to the enquirer himself making the Prasna; if planets in exaltationaspect the above Raasis, the knife belongs to one higher than himself; if planets in debilitation aspect the Raasis, the knife belongs to one higher than himself; and if planets posited in inimical houses aspect the above Raasis (Udaya, Aaroodha and Chhatra), the knife belongs to his enemy. 336

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सन्मुखो यदि खेटस्स्यात्तदीयं खड्गमुच्यते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तिर्यङमुखश्चेत्तच्छस्त्रमन्यदीयमितीरयेत्॥३३७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अधोमुखश्चेत्सङग्रामे च्युतमाहृतमुच्यते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तत्तच्चेष्टानुरूपेण स्वान्याहरणविस्मृतिः॥३३८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If forward–looking planets (the Moon and Jupiter,) aspect the Udaya, Aaroodha or Chhatra Raasis, the knife belongs to the owner (i.e. the person making the Prasna,). If the obliquely looking planet (Mars) aspects the above Raasis, the knife belongs to another; and if the downward–looking planets (Venus and Mercury) aspect the above Raasis, the knife has been obtained after defeating the foe, and the knife has fallen down and been picked up by the present owner. By taking into consideration the various characteristics of the planets, the ownership or misplacement of the knife is to be determined.  
 Note: This is explained in verses 40 and 50 earlier. 337–338

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681906921.png)

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

**Chapter XXII**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***OF SHADOWS AND SHAFTS***

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शल्यप्रश्ने तु तत्काले पादभा वसुनेत्रयुक्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अभ्यस्ता नृपसङ्ख्याभि शेषाणां फलमुच्यते॥३३९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 To answer some queries, the shadow of the person making the query is measured; and based, on its length certain calculations are made and predictions given. Measure the shadow, leaving the foot, by your pace, add 28, multiply by 12. and divide the sum by 16. The prediction is given on the basis of the quotient arrived at. This is called the Science of Salya. 339

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कपालास्थीष्टकालोष्टकाष्ठदेवविभूतयः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शावाङ्गारकधान्यानि धनपाषाणदर्दुराः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**गोस्थिश्वास्थिपिशाचाश्च ऋमाच्छत्यानि षोडश॥॥ ३४०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

*Salya is of 16 kinds. They are:*

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


(1) the skull (2) bone ( 3 ) brick ( 4 ) tile (5) firewood (6) god's idol (7) ash ( 8 ) corpse (9) charcocal (10) ghost (11) wealth (in terms of silver and gold ) ( 12 ) granite (13) toad (14) cow's bone ( 15 ) dog's bone, and (16) ghost. 340

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**एषु शल्येषु मण्ङूकस्वर्णगोस्थि च धान्यकम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**दृष्ट चेदुत्तमं चान्ये सर्वे स्युरशुभावहाः॥३४१॥**  

 Of these, if (10) (11) (13) and (14) come' together (i.e. grain, toad and cow's bone); it is reckoned as excellent (Uttama) since the 'Salya' grain is there. But other 'Salyas' are reckoned as bad, malefic.

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 An example is given here: The 'Salya' is determined by the quotient arrived at after the calculation given inverse 339. Let us take the length of the shadow as 16 paces. By adding 28, the sum is 44. Multiplied by 12, the product is 528. Divided by 16, the quotient is 33, remainder 0. Instead of 0 the remainder is taken as 16 as there are 16 'Salyas'. The 16th 'Salya' is 'ghost' ––which is bad or malefic. Let us take another example by measuring this shadow; we assume it is 13 paces. By the above calculation we get the final remainder 12. The 12th Salya is 'granite' which again is bad. By such calculations, if we arrive at the remainders, (10) (11) (13) or (14) i.e. 'grain', wealth, load or cows's bone, they are considered as being very good. 341

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अहिचक्रं प्रवक्ष्यामि यथासर्वज्ञभाषितम्।  
द्रव्यं शल्यं तथाशून्यं येन जानाति साधकः॥ ३४२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

What the wise men have stated as 'Ahi Chakra" I shall describe now. By this means, the student can learn about wealth, 'Salya' and 'Suunya' (i.e. Zero). 342

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ऊर्ध्वं रेखाष्टकं लेख्यं तिर्यक्पञ्च तथैव च।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अहिचक्रं भवेदेवमष्टाविंशतिकोष्ठकम्॥३४३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 The 'Ahi Chakra' is drawn thus by 8 lines vertically and 5 lines horizontally making 28 houses. 343

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अष्टाविंशतिकोष्ठेषु वहिधिष्ण्यादिकं न्यसेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**यत्र भे तिष्ठति शशी तत्र शाल्यमुदाहृतम्॥३४४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 These 28 houses have to be filled with the stars starting from Krittikaa. Wherever the Moon is found in these houses, it is to be noted there is 'Salya'. 344  

**उदयर्क्षादिकं न्यस्येदष्टाविंशतिकोष्ठके।  
गणयच्चन्द्रनक्षत्रं तत्र शल्यं प्रकीर्तितम्॥३४५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Taking the star rising in the horizon at the time of Prasna as the first, fill up the 28 houses with stars and counting the number up to the star where the Moon is, note the 'Salya' indicated by that number. 345

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**निधेर्निवर्तनैकस्थस्संभ्रान्तो यत्र भूतले।  
तत्र चक्रमिदं स्थाप्यं स्थानद्वारमुखस्थितम्॥३४६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

He, who is anxious to find treasure and is searching, should make the ‘Ahi Chakra' at that place of his search. 346

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

**![](../books_images/1681907468.png)**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तत्र पौष्णाश्वियाम्यर्क्षंकृत्तिकापितृभाग्यकम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उत्तराफल्गुनी लेख्यं पूर्वपङत्तयां भसप्तकम्॥३४७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Let him fill up the eastern 7 houses with the following stars (as shown in the figure above):

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 (1) Revatee (2) Aswinee (3) Bharanee (4) Krittikaa (5) Makha (6) Pubbaa (7) Uttaraa. 347

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अहिर्बुध्न्यादिपादर्क्षंशतभं ब्रह्मसार्पभम्।  
पुष्यहस्तं समालेख्यं द्वितीयां पङ्क्तिमास्थितम्॥३४८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 In the next seven, let him fill up the stars:

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 (1) Uttarabhadraa (2) Poorvabhadraa (3) Satabhisha (4) Rohinee (5) Aasleshaa (6) Poorvaashaadhaa and (7) Hasta. 348

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**विधि विष्णु धनिष्ठाख्यं सौम्यं रौद्र पुनर्वसू।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चित्राभान् च तृतीयायं पङ्कौ धिष्ण्यस्य सप्तकं॥३५९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 In the third seven, let him fill up the following stars:

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 (1) Abhijit (2) Sravana ( 3 ) Dhanishtha ( 4 ) Mrigasiraa (5) Aardraa (6) Punarvasu and (7) Chitta. 349

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**विश्वर्क्षं तोयभं मूलं ज्येष्ठामैत्रविशाखके।  
स्वाती पङ्क्तौ चतुर्थ्यां तु कृत्वा चक्रं विलेखयेत्॥ ३५०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 In the last line, the following stars are to be filled up:  
 (1) Uttaraashaadhaa ( 2 ) Poorvaashaadha (3) Moolaa (4) Jyeshthaa (5) Anuraadhaa ( 6 ) Visaakhaa and (7) Swaatee 350

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**एवं प्रजायते चक्रे प्रस्तारा पन्नगाकृतिः**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**द्वारशाखे मखायाम्ये द्वारस्था कृत्तिका मता॥३५१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Thus is formed the Ahi Chakra. Opposite the stars Bharanee and Makha rise two branches and in between is the hole opposite Krittikaa. In the Ahi Chakra the Moon is posited in 14 houses and the rest belongs to the Sun. 351

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अश्वीशपूर्वाषाढादित्रिकं पञ्च चतुष्टयम्।  
रेवतीपूर्वाभार्द्वेन्दोर्भान्यन्यानितु भास्वतः॥३५२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 As indicated in the figure, three stars from Aswinee, 5 stars from Aardraa, 4 stars from Poorvabhadraa and Revatee belong to the Moon i.e. Stars belonging to the Moon are: Aswince, Bharanee, Krittikaa, Aardraa, Punarvasu, Pushyami, Aasleshaa, Makha, Poorvabhadraa, Uttaraashaadhaa, Sravana, Dhanishthaa, Revatee and Poorvabhadraa. Stars belonging to the Sun are the remaining 14; Rohince, Mrigasiraa. Pubbaa, Uttara, Hasta, Chitta, Swaatee, Visaskhaa, Anuraadhaa, Jyeshthaa, Abhijit, Moolaa, Satabhisha and Uttarabhadraa. 352

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदयादिगता नाड्यो भग्नाः षष्ट्याप्तशेषके।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**दिनेन्दुभुक्तयुक्तोसौ भवेत्तत्कालचन्द्रमाः॥३५३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Find out the star where the Moon is at the time of Prasna and the time already gone in that star in terms of 'Naazhigai' (i.e. 24 minutes), multiply it by 25, and divide the product by 60. Leaving the quotient, the remainder is to be counted from the star where the Moon is, and the resulting star is called the 'dinentai". 353

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**षष्टिघ्नं तं निशानाथं शरवेदाप्तकं पुनः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**युगैश्शेषं भवेद्यत्तत्प्रागादिचक्रवर्गगम्।  
चन्द्रवत्साधयेत्सूर्यमृक्षस्थं चेष्टकालिकम्॥३५४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 Again taking the 'Naazhigai' already gone in that star by the Moon, multiply by 60 and divide by 45. The quotient is again to be divided by 4. The remainder indicates the direction in which the Moon will be station at the time of Prasna, taking East as 1, South as 2, West as 3 and North as 4.

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 Example: Let us take the Moon is in Mrigasiraa; it has already spent 52 Naazhigais there. Multiplying 52 by 27, the product is 1404, which divided by 60 gives the remainder 24. Counting 24 stars from Mrigasira, we get Aswinee. The Aswinee star is called dinendu. Again multiplying 52 (time already spent) by 60 and dividing it by 45, we get the remainder 1; it means, the Moon is in the East. Likewise the calculation is to be made for the Sun. 354

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पश्चाद्विलोकयेत्तौ च स्वर्क्षेवाचान्यभे स्थितौ।  
चन्द्रऋक्षे यदार्केन्दु निधिस्तत्र न संशयः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**भानुऋक्षे स्थितौ तौ चेत्तदा शल्यं च नान्यथा॥३५५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Having made the tabular statement as described in the above calculation, one has to find whether the Sun and the Moon are in their own cubicles or in each other's interchanged. If both the Sun and the Moon are in the Moon's cubicle, the person well get a treasure in that place. If both the Sun and the Moon are in the Sun's cubicle, the same Salya will be noted. If, however, it is otherwise, it means that there is no Salya in that place. 355

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्वस्वभद्वितयं ज्ञेयं नास्ति किञ्चिद्विपर्यये।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्थितं न लभते द्रव्यं चन्द्रं क्रूरग्रहान्विते॥३५६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If either the Sun or the Moon is in its own cubicle or both in their own cubicles, the Salya regarding treasure is to be calculated. If it is otherwise, it means there is no Salya. Even if the Moon is in its own house, but aspected by a malefic, the person will not get the treasure inspite of the fact of his having that desirable ‘Salya'. 356

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पुष्टे चन्द्रे भवेन्मुद्रा क्षीणे चन्द्रेऽल्पको निधिः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ग्रहदृष्टिवशात्सोऽपि विज्ञेयो नवधा वुधैः॥३५७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If it is a full Moon, the treasure will have a mudraa, (by this term, some infer that the treasure will be a large one), and if it is a partial Moon, the treasure will be meagre, if the Moon is aspected by the planet, the native of the treasure will be of 9 kinds 357

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**हेम तारं च ताम्रारं रत्नं कांस्यायसं त्रपु।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नागं चन्द्रे विजानीयाद्भास्करादिग्रहेक्षिते॥३५८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon arrived at by calculation, is aspected by the Sun, the treasure will be gold. But this Moon is aspected by the Moon at the time of Prasna, the treasure will be silver or pearl; if the Moon is aspected by Mars, the treasure will be copper; if aspected by Mercury, it will be brass; if by Jupiter, the treasure will be gems; if by Venus, it will be bronze; if by Saturn it will be iron; if by Rahu it will be lead; and if by Ketu it will be tin. 358

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मिश्रैमिंश्रं भवेद्द्रव्यं शून्यं दृष्टिविपर्यये।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सर्वग्रहेक्षिते चन्द्रे निर्दिष्टोऽसौ महानिधिः॥३५९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is aspected by two or more planets, the treasure also will be of a mixed character. If no planet aspects the Moon, the treasure too will be nothing. But if all plane aspect the Moon, the treasure will be a very large one. 359

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुभक्षेत्रगते चन्द्रे लाभस्स्यान्नात्र संशयः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पापक्षेत्रे न लाभोहि विज्ञेयः खगपारगैः॥३६०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is in beneficial sign, there will be gain of treasure. But if it is in a malefic sign, there will be no gain, say those experts in this Science of Salya. 360  

**हेम तारं च ताम्ररं पाषाणां मृण्मयायसम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सूर्यादिगृहगे चन्द्रे द्रव्यभाण्डं प्रजायते॥३६१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is in the Sun's house the treasure will be in a golden vessel; if the Moon is in its own sign, the vessel will be of silver or pearl; if in Mars' house it will be a copper vessel; if in Mercury's sign, the vessel will be of bronze; if in Jupiter's sign it will be stone vessel; if in Venus's sign, it will be a mudpot; if in Saturn's house it will be an iron vessel. 361

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**भुक्तराश्यंशमानेन भूमानं कोविदैः करैः।  
नीचे विघ्नं परं नीचे जलस्थोऽसौ भवेन्निधिः॥ ३६२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 The size of the plot of ground where the treasure is found can be determined by the 'amsas' (strength) in the Moon's sign or by the strength of rays in the planets in that sign. If the Moon is in a debilitated amsa, the treasure will be under water. 362

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्वोचस्थ ऊध्वेगं द्रव्यं नवांशक क्रमेण च।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**परमोच्चे परे तुङ्गे भित्तिस्थं त्वृक्षसंक्रमे॥३६३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is in its own exaltation sign, or in exalted amsa the treasure will be found easily in the upper layer. If the Moon is in its highest exaltation, the treasure will be in still higher layers; and if the Moon is in the junction of the signs, the treasure will be inside a wall. 363

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चन्दांशभुक्तमानेन द्रव्यसङ्ख्या विधीयते।  
तस्या दशगुणा वृद्धिः षड्वर्गेन्दुबलक्रमात्॥३६४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 The 16 kinds of Salyas are determined according to the strength of the cubicle in which the Moon dwells. The Shadvargas of the Moon give added strength and the number obtained by ordinary reckoning is increased tenfold. 364

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**ग्रहो सुखं ग्रहश्चैव क्षेत्रपालञ्च मातृकाः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**र्दापेशं भीषणं रुद्रं पक्षं नागं विदुः क्रमात्॥३६५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Of this tenfold increase, the first increase is related to the planet concerned; the 2nd to the face; the 3rd to the planet; the 4th to the guardian of the field (Kshetrapaala); the 5th to the divine mothers; the 6th to the bright luminous gods; the 7th to the terrifying gods; the 8th to Rudra; the 9th to Yaksha; and the 10th to the Naagas. 365

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**यहे होमः प्रकर्तव्यो सुखे नारायणो बलिः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**क्षेत्रपाले सुरां मांसं मातृकायां महाबलिः॥३६६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 For the 1st increase, a ‘homa' sacrifice is to be done; for the 2nd increase, the Naaraayana sacrifice is to be performed; in the 3rd, an ordinary sacrifice is to be done; in the 4th increase, meat and wine are to be offered; in the Sth increase, a big sacrifice must be made. 366 
                            
**दीपेशे दीपजा पूजा भीषणे भीषणार्चनम्।  
रुद्रे च रुद्रजो जाप्यो यक्षे यक्षादिशान्तयः॥ ३६७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 In the 6th increase regarding luminous gods the worship of lights is to be performed; in the 7th the worship of the frightful gods is to be done; in the 8th, one has to recite the mantras of Rudra; in the 9th the Yakshas have to be appeased by appropriate measures. 367

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नागे नागग्रहाः पूज्या गणनाथेन संयुताः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**लक्ष्मीधरदितत्वानि सर्वकार्येषु पूजयेत्॥३६८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 In the 10th increase, worship to the serpentgods associated with the lord of the elementals (Gananaatha) is to be preformed. In every kind of worship, prayer to wealth–giving elementals is also to be offered. 368

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**एवं कृते विधाने हि निरसाध्योपि सिद्ध्यति॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**निधिप्राप्त्या नरा लोके वन्दनीया न संशयः॥३६९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 By doing such rituals, even the impossible kinds of work can be accomplished. Undoubtedly people respect those who have obtained treasure. 369

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शङ्कास्थलस्य विस्तारायामावन्योन्यताडितौ।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**विंशत्यापहृतं शेषमरत्निरिति कीर्तितम्॥३७०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**रनिं गुणित्वा नवभि र्निरिसन्तानमुच्यते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तत्प्रदेशं गुणित्वाङ्कै र्हृत्वा विंशतिभिर्यदि॥३७१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**शिष्टं अंगुलं एवोक्तं रत्नि प्रादेशं अंगुलं।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**एवं क्रमेण रत्न्याद्यं अगाधं कथयेदघः॥३७२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


* Sishtam Angulam Eyvouktam*

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

* Ratni Praadesam Angulam  
 Eyvam Krameyna Ratnyaadyam  
 Agaagham Kathayeydagha :\।*

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The length and breadth of the reckoned place must first be determined. By multiplying one by the other and dividing the product by 20, the quotient obtained is called Aratni. The remainder is to be multiplied by nine and the product is called Nirisantaanam. Multiplying this again by nine and dividing it by 20, the quotient is to be left out, and the remainder is to be taken as Angula. This is called Ratnipraadesamangulam. This is the method by which the exact place of the treasure inside the earth in terms of Aratni and Angula is determined. 370–372

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**केन्द्रेषु पापयुक्तेषु पृष्टं शल्य न दृश्यते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुभग्रहयुतेष्वेषु शल्यं तत्र प्रजायते।  
पापसौम्ययुते केन्द्रे शल्यमस्तीति निर्दिशेत्॥३७३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If malefics are in the Kendras, the ascertained Salya cannot be found out. But if benefics are posited in the Kendras, the Salya will be found there. But if both benefics and malefics are in the Kendras, one can only predict that the Salya is there. 373

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**रविः पश्यति चेद्देवं कुजश्चेब्दह्मराक्षसम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**केन्द्रे चन्द्रारसहिते कुजनक्षत्रकोष्ठके॥३७४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**पिपीलिकाघः केन्द्रे तु जीवचन्द्रसमन्विते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जीवस्थेडुगते कोठे स्वर्णं गोपुरुषास्थिनी॥३७५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Sun aspects a Kendra prediction is about gods; if Mars aspects the Kendra one that to refer to Brahmarakshasas (devils). If both Mars and the Moon are in a Kendra, and it happens to be the trough of a star belonging to Mars, one can find in the earth, only an ant–hill. If Jupiter and the Moon are in a Kendra and it happens to be a trough of a star belonging to Jupiter one can find in the earth either gold or the bones of a cow or man. 374–375  

**उदयारूढकेन्द्रेषु स्वर्भानुर्यदि तिष्ठति।  
राहुस्थर्क्षगते कोष्ठे वल्मीकमुपदीपयुक्॥३७६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Rahu is in Udaya or Aaroodha Kendra and it happens to be the trough of a star belonging to Rahu, one has to predict the unearthing of an ant–hill with light nearby. 376

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**शुभान् केन्द्रे युतान् पापाः पश्यन्ति बलिनो यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तत्क्षेत्रे विद्यते शल्यमेषु पापाः यदि स्थिताः॥३७७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If benefic planets in a Kendra are aspected by strong malefics, one can predict a Salya (bone) in that place. 377

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**देवयक्षपिशाचाद्यास्तत्र तिष्ठन्त्यसंशयम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ग्रहांशुसङ्ख्यया तेषां खातमानं वदेत्सुधीः॥३७८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If malefics are in Kendras, there is no doubt that in that place there will be ghosts, Yakshas or gods. In accordance with the number of rays of the planets will be these ghosts or gods down deep in the earth. 378

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**चन्द्रे बुधेन संयुक्ते वुधनक्षत्रकोष्ठगे।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्वशल्यं विद्यते तत्र केन्द्रे शुकेन्दुसंयुते॥३७९॥  

शुक्रस्थितर्क्षगे कोष्ठे रौप्यं श्वेतशिलापिवा।  
पञ्चषडसुभूतानि सपादैकं तथैव च॥३८०॥  

सार्धरूपाक्षिरवयः सूर्यादीनां करास्स्मृताः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शल्यागाधमनेनैव करेण कथयेत्सुधीः॥३८१॥**  

 If Mars and Mercury are in the trough of a star belonging to Mercury there will be found a 'Salya' associated with Mercury. If Venus and the Moon are in a Kendra which is the trough of a star belonging to Venus, there will be found silver or white stone. The Sun, the Moon, Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus, Saturn, Rahu and Ketu are respectively having 5,6,8, 5, 1¼, 1¼, 1½, 2 and 12 rays. In terms of these rays, one has to dig deep in the earth to find the Salya. 379–381

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681967786.png)  
**Chapter XXIII**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***OF WELLS***

</div>

<div>


**अथ वक्ष्ये विशेषेण कूपखाते विनिर्णयम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आयामे त्वष्टरेखाः स्युस्तिर्यग्रेखास्तु पञ्चच।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**एवङ्कृते भवेत्कोष्ठमष्टाविंशति सङ्ख्यकम्॥३८२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**प्रभाते प्राङ्मुखं कृत्वा कोष्टेष्वेतेषु वुद्धिमान्।  
ऐश्ये कोष्ठद्वयं त्यक्त्वा तृतीयादिषु च क्रमात्।  
कृत्तिकादित्रयं न्यस्य रौद्रञ्च तदधो न्यसेत्॥ ३८३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**तदुत्तरत्रयेष्वेव पुनर्वस्वादिकं त्रयम्।  
तत्पश्चिमादियाम्येषु यथा चित्रावसानकम्॥३८४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**तत्कोष्ठपूर्वयोः स्वातिविशाखे न्यस्य तत्परम्।  
प्रदक्षिणक्रमादग्निनक्षत्रान्ताश्च तारकाः॥३८५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**मध्याह्लाद्दक्षिणाशास्यं पश्चिमास्यं निशामुखात्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चक्रमालोकयेद्विद्वान् रात्र्यर्धादुत्तराननम्॥३८६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 Now I will tell you calculations about digging wells. Draw five lines across and 8 vertically (as stated in verse 346) forming 38 troughs or cubicles.The stars have to be filled up taking that particular star at the time of Prasna as the first. If it is morning, the cubicles have to face East first; if the Prasna is made at noontime, the cubicles of the South are to face forward; if the Prasna is made in the evening, the cubicles have to face West first; if it is made after mid–night, the cubicles have to face North first as in the following diagrams: 382–386

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**मध्याह्ने पैत्रमारभ्य मैत्रमाद्यं निशामुखे।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अर्धरात्रेधनिष्ठाद्यं पूर्ववद्गणयेत्क्रमात्॥३८७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**आग्रेय्यां दिशि नैर्ऋत्यां वायव्यां कोष्ठकद्वयम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**त्यक्त्वा प्रत्येकमेवं हि तृतीयाद्यं विलोकयेत्॥३८८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Prasna is made at noon, leave out two troughs (cubicles) in the south–east and from the third beginning with Makha star fill up the rest as in the earlier table. If the Prasna is made in the evening, leave out two troughs (cubicles) in the south–west and from the third beginning with Anuraadha, fill up the rest with stars as in the earlier table. If the Prasna is made in the midnight, leave out the first two troughs (cubicles) in the north–east and from the third commencing with dhanishthaa, fill up the rest with stars as earlier. 387–388

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**दिनार्धं सप्तभिर्हृत्वा यल्लब्धं नाडिकादिकम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ज्ञात्वा तत्तत्प्रमाणेन कृत्तिकादीनि विन्यसेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**यन्नक्षत्रं तदा सिद्धं प्रश्रकाले विशेषतः॥३८९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The length of half a day is to be divided among 7 stars commencing from Krittikaa and they have to be filled up in the cubicles as in Table 1: e.g., If a day is taken as 29 Naazhigais (24 minutes make one Naazhigai); half a day comes to 14%, and if this is divided by 7 we get for each star 2 Vs Naazhigais Which means 51 minutes. For the first 51 minutes from 6 a.m. if the Prasna is made, we. have to take the star as Krittikaa. Likewise we have to know which of the 7 stars is reigning at the time of Prasna, between 6 a.m. to 12 Noon. 389

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**कृत्तिकास्थानमारभ्य पूर्ववद्गणयेत्सुधीः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**यत्कोष्ठे चन्द्रनक्षत्रं तत्रोदयक्रमाल्लिखेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तदादीनि क्रमेणैव पूर्ववद्गुणयेत्सुधीः॥३९०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 In a similar manner, from 12 Noon to 6 p.m., the 7 stars from Makha to Visaakhaa are ruling, each for 51 minutes.  
 From 6 p.m. to 12 midnight, the 7 stars Anuraadhaa to Dhanishthaa are ruling, each for 51 minutes; and one has to find out which star is to be considered at the time of Prasna.; From midnight to 6 in the moming, the 7 stars from Satabhisha to Bharanee are to be taken, and calculations accordingly made.  
 Further at the time of Prasna, one has to determine the star of the day according to the almanac, and fix it up in the cubicle, starting from Anuraadhaa if it is night from 6 to 12,and from Dhanishthaa if it is morning from 12 midnight to 6 a.m. That cubicle is called the house of the Moon's star. 389–390  

**यत्रेन्दुदृश्यते तत्र समृद्धमुदकं भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुक्रनक्षत्रकोष्ठे वा जलमस्तीत्युदाहरेत्॥३९१॥  

जीवनक्षत्रकोष्ठेतु तत्र स्वर्णमुदीरयेत्।  
तुलोक्षकर्ककुंभालिमीननक्राश्च राशयः॥३९२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**जलरूपा स्तदुदये जलमस्तीति निर्दिशेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तत्रस्थौ चन्द्रशुक्रौ चेदस्ति तत्र बहूदकम्॥३९३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 Having constructed this, where the Moon is situated (namely the house of the Moon's star), it has to be noted that it is a watery place. If the cubicle happens to have a star associated with Venus, one has to predict that the place is watery. If the star happens to be associated with Jupiter, one can predict the finding of gold there.  
 The signs of Libra, Taurus, Cancer, Aquarius, Scorpio and Capricorn are stated to be watery signs. If the star happens to rise in any one of these watery signs, prediction about water being available (for digging wells) in that place should be made. If, in that place, the Moon and Venus are posited, prediction about a great volume of water can be made. 391–393

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**बुधजीवोदये तत्र किञ्चिज्जलमुदीरयेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**एतान् राशीन् प्रपश्यन्ति यदि शन्यर्क भूमिजाः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जलं न विद्यते तत्र फणिदृष्टे बहूदकम्॥३९४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If that rising sign belongs to the Mercury group, a little water can be predicted. But if Saturn or Sun aspects the above signs, there will be no water. If Rahu aspects them, there willbe water. 394  

**अधस्तादुदयारूढात्तच्छत्रेतूपरि स्थिते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जलग्रहयुते दृष्टे चाधश्चेत्स्यादधोजलम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ऊर्ध्वदृष्टिर्ग्रहो राशावूर्ध्वमेवोदकं भवेत्॥३९५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Chhatra Raasi is above the Udaya and Aaroodha Raasis, and is aspected by a watery plane or associated with it, water will be found at a deep level. But if an upward–looking planet is in that Raasi, the water can be found at a higher level.  
 Note: The planets in the six signs commencing from that where the Sun is posited are called upward–looking planets. The planets after the six signs (i.e. from the 7th to the 12th) are called downward–looking planets. 395

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ऊर्ध्वाधः स्थलयोः पापास्तिष्ठन्ति यदि नोदकम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अधो जलं चतुस्स्थानादस्तान्नद्यागमो भवेत्॥३९६॥**  

 If malefics are found either above or below the Udaya Aaroodha and Chhatra Raasis, there will be no water in that place. But if a malefic is in the 4th place from Udaya or Aaroodha signs, water will be found at a deep level. 396

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**दशमे नवमे वर्षे केचिदाहुर्मनीषिणः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जलाजलग्रहवशाज्जलनिर्णयमीरयेत्॥३९७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Some astrologists predict that a river will flow in that place after 7 or 10 years. The availability of water is to be determined by finding out watery or non–watery planets in the place. 397

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**केन्द्रषु तिष्ठतश्चन्द्रजीवौ यदि शुभोदकम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चन्द्रे शुक्रयुते केन्द्रे पर्वतेऽपि जलं वदेत्॥३९८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon or Jupiter is posited in a Kendra, good potable water is available there. If Venus and the Moon are in a Kendra, water will be in plenty even if it happens to be a mountainous place. 398

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चन्द्रसौम्ययुते केन्द्रे जीर्णञ्च लवणोदकम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आरूढात् केन्द्रगे चन्द्रे परिध्याद्यभिवीक्षिते॥३९९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Moon and Mercury are in a Kendra, old salt water will be available in that place. If the Moon is in a Kendra to the Aaroodha Lagna and is aspected by Parivesha or other Upagrahas, water will be at a deep level. 399

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अधो जलं ततोगाधं पूर्वोक्तग्रहरश्मिभिः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुक्रेण सौम्यो युक्तश्चेत्कषायं जलमादिशेत्॥४००॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 The depth in which water will be available is determined by counting the rays of the respective planets detailed above. If Mercury and Venus are associated and posited in a Kendra the water will be brackish. 400

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कन्यामिथुनभे सौम्ये जलं स्यादन्तरालगम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**वृहस्पतौ राहुयुते पाषाणो जायतेऽन्तरा॥४०१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Water will be at a middle level (neither too high nor too low), if Mercury is in its own signs of Gemini or Virgo. If Jupiter is associated with Rahu, granite stones will be in the middle level. 401

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुक्रचन्द्रयुते राहावगाधे जलमेधते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**भास्करे क्षारसलिलं परिवेषे धनुर्यदि।  
राहुणा संयुते मन्दे जलं स्यादन्तरालगम्॥४०२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Rahu is associated with Venus and the Moon, there will be gush of water at a deep level. If the Sun or Parivesha is there in Sagittarius, the water will be salty in taste. If Saturn is associated with Rahu, water will be available at a middle level. 402

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**अर्कस्योषरभूमिस्स्यात्पापाद्वा कंटकस्थली।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नारिकेलादिपुन्नागपूगयुक्ता क्षमा गुरोः॥४०३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**शुक्रस्य कदली वल्ली बुधस्य पनसो भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**वल्मीकं राहुकेत्वोश्च त्वितिज्ञात्वा वदेद्बुधः॥४०४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The kind of soil a place would be, where one wants to dig a well is determined thus. If the Sun is there, the soil would be barren with saline content; the malefics–Saturn and Mars–indicate a soil where only thorns and brambles can grow. Jupiter indicates coconut, dates and arecanut groves; Venus indicates plantain and creeper–growing expanse; Mercury points to jack–fruit–growing soil; Rahu and Ketu indicate anthills. 403–404

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681969978.png)

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681970139.png)

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681970276.png)

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681970434.png)

</div>

<div>


**शनिराहूदये काष्ठोरगवल्मीकदर्शनम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्वामिदृष्टियुते वापि स्वक्षेत्रमिति कीर्तयेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अन्यैर्युक्तेऽथवा दृष्टे परकीयस्थलं वदेत्॥४०५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Saturn or Rahu is posited in Udaya Lagna at the place where one wants to dig a well, one can only meet with termites, snakes and other insects. If the rising Lagna sign is aspected by the lord of the Lagna, the place where the well is being dug is owned by the person; but if it is either aspected by or associated with other planets, the place belongs to another. 405

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681970550.png)  
**Chapter XXIV**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***OF ARMIES***

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सैन्यस्यागमनं वक्ष्ये शत्रोरागमनं तथा।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चरोदये चरारूढे पापाः पंचमगा यदि॥४०६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Now I will describe the arrival of armies and the entry of the enemy into the country. He who knows the Prasna Saastra must predict about the arrival of armies, if the Udaya Raasi and the Aaroodha Raasi happen to be in a moveable sign and malefics are in the 5th house. 406

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सेनागमनमस्तीति कथयेच्छास्त्रवित्तमः।  
चतुष्पादुदयेजाते युग्मराश्युदये तथा॥४०७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Udaya Raasi happens to be in a quadruped or biped sign and the lord of the Lagna is in retrograde motion; the army will return to its country. 407

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**लग्नस्याधिपतौ वक्रे सेना पथि निवर्तते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शत्रोरागमनं नास्ति चतुर्थे पापसंयुते॥४०८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The enemy will not invade the country, if a malefic is positedin the 4th house. 408

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदयारूढछत्रेषु केन्द्रेषु भुजगो यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**दूरस्थिता च नायाति सेना पथि निवर्तते॥४०९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Rahu happens to be in Udaya, Aaroodha or Chhatra Raasi, or in Kendra, the army will be far away. It will not enter the town. It will return home, while it is half way. 409

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आरूढे ह्युदिताः कुंभकुलीरालिझषा यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चतुर्थकेन्द्रे बलिनो यदि सेना निवर्तते॥४१०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Aaroodha Raasi happens to be in any one of the signs Aquarius, Cancer, Scorpio, or Pisces, and if in there 4th place (Kendra) there is a strong planet, the enemy's forces will retreat and return home. 410

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चरोदये चरारूढे भौमार्कगुरवस्तदा।  
तिष्ठन्ति यदि पश्यन्ति सेना याति महत्तरा॥४११॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Udaya Raasi rises in a moveable sign, and happens to be also the Aaroodha Raasi, and if Mars, the Sun or Jupiter is posited there, or aspects the Raasis, prediction about the arrival of a big army should be made.  
* Note* : The oncoming army is called 'yaayee', and the invaded army is called the 'sthaayee'. 411

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आरूढे स्वामिमित्रोच्चग्रहयुक्तेऽथ वीक्षिते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्थायिनो विजयं ब्रूयाद्यायिनो भङ्गमादिशेत्॥४१२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the lord of the Aaroodha Raasi, or the friend of that lord is associated with or aspected by an exalted planet, the' sthaayee' will be victorious and the 'yaayee' will return home defeated. 412

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**एवं छत्रे विशेषोऽस्ति विपरीते जयो भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**यायी बलं समायाति छत्रे बलसमन्विते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आरूढे बलसंयुक्ते स्थायी विजयमाप्नुयात्॥४१३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 But there is a speciality in the case of the Chhatra Raasi, where the result will be the reverse of the above, i.e. if the Chhatra Raasi is strong, the yaayee will be triumphant. But in the case of the Aaroodha Raasi being strong, he will be firm in his own stand; i.e. the sthaayee will be able to defeat the yaayee. 413

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**आरूढे नीचरिपुभिर्ग्रहैर्युक्तेऽथ वीक्षिते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्थायी परगृहीतस्स्याच्छत्रेष्वेवं विपर्ययः॥४१४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Aaroodha Raasi is debilitated, or associated with or aspected by a malefic, the sthaayee will be captured by the enemy. But if the Chhatra Raasi is in a similar situation, the reverse will happen; *i.e*. the sthaayee will be triumphant, and the enemy will be defeated. 414

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**शुभोदये तु पूर्वाह्णे यायिनो विजयो भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुभोदये तु सायाह्ने स्थायी विजयमाप्नुयात्॥४१५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If a benefic is in the Udaya Raasi in the forenoon, the enemy will succeed. But in the evening, if a benefic is in the Udaya Raasi, the sthaayee will succeed. 415

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**छत्रारूढोदये वापि क्रूरांशे पापसंयुते।  
तत्काले पृच्छतां सद्यः कलहो जायते महान्॥४१६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Chhatra Raasi, Udaya Raasi or Aaroodha Raasi happens to be fierce or associated with a malefic, prediction has to be made that there will be a fierce battle imminent for the sthaayee. 416

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पृष्ठोदये तथारूढे पापैर्युक्तेऽथ वीक्षिते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**दशमे पापसंयुक्ते चतुष्पादुदयेऽपि वा।  
कलहो जायते शीघ्रं सन्धिस्स्याच्छुभवीक्षिते॥४१७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Aaroodha Raasi happens to be a Prushthodaya (rising by the hinder part) and is associated with or aspected by a malefic, or a malefic is posited in the 10th place, or if the Udaya Raasi is quadruped sign, conflict will soon arise. If what is stated above is aspected by a benefic, amity and friendship will take place. 417

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**उदयादिषु षट्केषु शुभा राशिषु चेत्स्थिताः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्थायिनो विजयं ब्रूयादूर्ध्वंचेद्यायिनो जयः॥४१८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पापग्रहयुते व्यस्तं मिश्रे सन्धिः प्रजायते।  
उभयत्र स्थिताः पापा बलवन्तस्समो जयः॥४१९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the six signs from the Udaya Raasi are occupied by benefics, the sthaayee will be triumphant. But if benefics are in signs beyond the six adjacent to the Udaya Raasi, the yaayee will succeed. That is, if the six signs adjacent to the Udaya Raasi are malefics, the sthaayee will be defeated, the yaayee will succeed. But if the malefics are beyond the six signs, the yaayee will be defeated, and the sthaayee will be triumphant. But if both the malefics and benefics are mixed in these signs, friendship will ensue between the two parties. If strong malefics are on either side of the Lagna, *i.e*. in the 2nd and 12th places, the two rival parties will be equal; i.e. the enemy will have scored some successes and the sthaayee some successes. 418–419

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तुर्यादिराशिभिः षड्भिरागतस्य फलं वदेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तदन्यराशिभिः षड्भिः स्थायिनः फलमादिशेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**एवं ग्रहस्थितिवशात्पूर्ववत्कथयेद्बुधः॥४२०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The strength of the parties has to be assessed thus: The strength of the six signs from the 4th Raasi from Udaya sign determines the enemy's strength; while the six other Raasis beyond give the strength of the yaayee. Thus is prediction to be made in terms of the relative strengths of the planets. 420

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ग्रहोदये विशेषोऽस्ति शन्यर्काङ्गारकोदये।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आगतस्य जयं ब्रूयात्स्थायिनो भङ्गमादिशेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**बुधशुक्रोदये, यायी जयी चन्द्रगुरूदये॥४२१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 Now the effects of planets being in the Udaya Raasi will be described : If at the time of Prasna, Saturn, the Sun or Mars is in Udaya Raasi, success will go to the enemy. If Mercury and Venus are in Udaya Lagna, the sthaayee will be defeated. 421

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पञ्चषड्लाभरिःफेषु तिग्मांशुः संस्थितो यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आगतः स्त्रीधनादीनि हृत्वा वस्तूनि गच्छति॥४२२॥**  


</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon or Jupiter is in the Lagna, the enemy will be successful. If the Sun is in the 5th 6th, 11th or 12th place, the enemy will go away, capturing women, wealth and property. 422

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**द्वितीये दशमे सौरिर्यदि सेनासमागमः।  
यदि शुक्रः स्थितः षष्ठे योज्यं संधिर्भविष्यति॥४२३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Saturn is in the 2nd or 10th place from the Prasna Lagna, there will be clash of arms. If Venus is in the 6th place, there will be peace or settlement. 423

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चतुर्थे पञ्चमे शुक्रो यदि तिष्ठति तत्क्षणात्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्त्रीघनादीनि वस्तूनि यायी दत्वा प्रयास्यति॥४२४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Venus is in the 4th or 5th place, the yaayee will give away women and property to the enemy and run away defeated. 424  

**सप्तमे शुक्रसंयुक्ते स्थायी भवति दुर्बलः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नवाष्टसप्तसहजादन्यत्र हि कुजो यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्थायी विजयमाप्नोति परसेना समागमे॥४२५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Venus is in the 7th place, the sthaayee will be weak. If Mars is anywhere except the 9th, 8th, 7th and 3rd places, the sthaayee will fight against the enemy and be successful. 425

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चतुर्थे पञ्चमे चन्द्रे स्थायी च विजयी भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तृतीये पञ्चमे भानौ यदि सेनासमागमः॥४२६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is in the 4th or 5th place the sthaayee will definitely succeed. If the Sun is in the 3rd or 5th place, there will be clash of arms. 426

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मित्रस्थाने स्थिते संधिर्नोचेत्स्थायी जयी भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चतुर्थे वित्तदः स्थायी षष्ठे चेत्स्थायिनो मृतिः॥४२७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Sun is in a friend's sign, there will be settlement between the two parties. Otherwise, the sthaayee will succeed. If the Sun is in the 4th place, the sthaayee will give away property to the enemy. If the Sun is in the 6th place, the sthaayee will die. 427

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**उदयात्सहजे सौम्ये द्वितीये यदि भास्करः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्थायिनो विजयं ब्रूयाद्वयत्यस्ते यायिनो जयः॥४२८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Mercury is in the 3rd place from the Lagna and the Sun in the 2nd place, the sthaayee will succeed. If it were the reverse, the enemy would succeed. 428

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ससौम्ये भास्करे माते समयुद्धं वदेद्बुधः।  
लग्नात्पञ्चमगे सौम्ये यायी भवति चार्थदः।  
द्वित्रस्थे सोमजे यायी विजयी भवति ध्रुवम्॥। ४२९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Sun and Mercury are together, there will be ceaseless war between the two parties. If Mercury is in the 5th place, the yaayee will give away property to the sthaayee. But if Mercury is in the 2nd and 3rd places, the yaayee will definitely succeed. 429

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**एकादशे व्यये सौम्ये स्थायी विजयमेष्यति।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**एकादशेऽर्के यायी तु हतस्त्रीबान्धवो भवेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शत्रुनीचस्थिते सूर्ये स्थायिनो भङ्गमादिशेत्॥४३०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Mercury is in the 11th or 12th place, the sthaayee will be triumphant. If the Sun is in the 11th place the yaayee's women and relatives will be killed. If the Sun is in inimical or debi–litated signs, the sthaayee will be defeated. 430

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**उदयात्पञ्चमभ्रातृव्ययेषु धिषणो यदि।  
यायी भङ्गं समायाति द्वितीये संधिरुच्यते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**दशमैकादशे जीवो यदि याय्यर्थदो भवेत्॥। ४३१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Jupiter is in the 5th, 3rd or 12th places from the Udaya Lagna,–the yaayee will be defeated. If Jupiter is in the 2nd place, there will be settlement between the parties. If Jupiter is in the 10th or 11 th place, the yaayee will give away property. 431  

**चन्द्रादित्यौसमस्थाने संधिस्स्यात्तिष्ठतो यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**विपरीते तु युद्धं स्याद्धानोर्द्वादशगे विधौ।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तत्र युद्धं न भवति शास्त्रे ज्ञानप्रदीपके॥४३२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Sun and the Moon are neutral signs, there will be truce and the parties will settle their differences. If it were the reverse, there will be war between the two. If the Moon is in the 12th place to the Sun, there will be no war, says the science of ‘JNAANAPRADEEPIKAA'. 432

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चरराशिस्थिते चन्द्रे चरराश्युदयेपि वा।  
शत्रुरागत्य संधाता विपरीते विपर्ययः॥४३३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is in a moveable sign or a movable sign is rising, the enemy will seek peace. If it is the reverse, the effect too will be reverse. 433

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**युग्मराशिस्थिते चन्द्रे स्थिरराश्युदये तथा।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अर्द्धराज्यं समागत्य सेनानीर्विनिवर्तते॥४३४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is in an odd sign and a fixed sign is rising, the enemy's commander–in–chief will come halfway into the sthaayee's kingdom and then return home. 434

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सिह्मादिराशिषट्के तु स्थायिनो भङ्गदायकः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कर्कादिव्युत्क्रमात्षट्के यायिनश्चन्द्रमास्थितः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्थायीयायीक्रमेणैवं ब्रूयाद्ग्रहवशात्फलम्॥४३५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is in Leo, Virgo, Libra, Scorpio, Sagittarius and Capricom, the sthaayee will meet only with defeats. But if it is in the other six signs, namely, from Aquarius to Can– cer, the yaayee will be defeated.  
Thus is prediction about success or defeat to the parties made by the position of the planets. 435

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681974213.png)

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


**Chapter**XXV**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***ON TRAVEL***

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**यात्राकाण्डं प्रवक्ष्यामि सर्वेषां हितलिप्सया।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**गमनागमनं चैव लाभालाभौ शुभाशुभम्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सर्वं विचार्यकथयेत्पृच्छतां शास्त्रवित्तमः॥४३६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 In the interest of all, I am now describing the auspicious time for travel. After properly examining the details about going, coming, gain, loss, good and bad, the Prasna is to be answered. 436  

**मित्रक्षेत्राणि पश्यन्ति यदि मित्रग्रहास्तदा।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**मित्रस्यागमनं ब्रूयान्नीचं नीचग्रहा यदि॥४३७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If friendly planets aspect the friendly signs at the time of Prasna, the arrival of friends is to be predicted. Likewise if weak planets aspect weak signs the arrival of lowly persons is to be expected. 437

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नीचस्यागमनं ब्रूयादुच्चमुच्चग्रहा यदि।  
स्वाधिकाराय गमनं पुंराशौ पुंग्रहा यदि॥४३८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If exalted planets aspect the exalted signs, the person'stravel on official duty is to be predicted. 438

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**पुरुषायेति गमनं स्त्रीराशौ सीग्रहा यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्त्रियै गमनमित्युक्त मन्येष्वेवं विचारयेत्॥४३९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If male planets are in male signs the travel is in relation to some work with a man; and if female planets are in female signs, the travel is in connection with a woman. Such events are to be expected in other places too. 439

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चरराश्युदयारूढे तत्तद्ग्रहविलोकिते।  
तत्तदाशासु गच्छन्ति प्रष्टारः शास्त्रनिर्णयः॥ ४४०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Udaya and Aaroodha Raasis are moveable signs and are aspected by various planets, travel will be in the direction of the respective planets. 440

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्थिरराश्युदयारूढे शन्यर्काङ्गारकाः स्थिताः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अथवा दशमस्थाश्चेद्गमनागमने न च॥४४१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Udaya and Aaroodha Raasis are fixed and if Saturn, the Sun and Mars are posited there or in the 10th house, neither arrival nor departure will take place. 441

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुक्रसौम्येन्दुजीवाश्च तिष्ठन्ति चरराशिषु।  
विद्यते स्वेष्टसिध्यर्थं गमनागमनं तदा॥४४२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Venus, Jupiter and the Moon are in moveable signs, travel will take place only in one's own interest. 442

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**स्थितिप्रश्ने स्थिति ब्रूयान्मस्तकोदयराशिषु।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पृष्ठोदयेषु गमनं क्रमेण शुभदं वदेत्॥४४३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Prasna is in connection with travel, if the rising sign is Sirshodaya (head rising,), there will be no travel, and if the Prishthodaya sign is rising, there will be travel, which will be beneficial. 443

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**द्वितीये च तृतीये च तिष्ठन्ति यदि पुंग्रहाः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**त्रिदिनात्पत्रिकायाति दूतो वा प्रेषितस्य च॥४४४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If a male planet is in the 2nd or 3rd place from the Prasna Lagna, a letter will come with in three days; or a messenger will come from the person who has gone on travel. 444  

**लग्नार्थसहजव्योमलाभेष्विन्दुज्ञभार्गवाः।  
तिष्ठन्ति यदि तत्काले त्वावृत्तिः प्रेषितस्य च॥४४५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon, Mercury or Venus is in the 1st, 2nd, 3rd, 10th or 11th place, the man who has been sent out will returnsoon. 445

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**चतुर्थे द्वादशे वापि तिष्ठन्तश्चेच्छुभग्रहाः।  
पत्रिका प्रेषितस्याशु समायाति न संशयः॥४४६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If benefits are in the 4th or 12th place, a letter from the man who has gone out will definitely come. 446

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**षष्ठे वा पञ्चमे वापि यदि पापग्रहाः स्थिताः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**प्रेषितो व्याधिपीडार्तः समायाति न संशयः॥४४७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If malefics are in the 6th or 5th place from the Prasna Lagna, the man who has gone out will return with sickness. 447  

**चापोक्षछागसिंहेषु यदि तिष्ठति चन्द्रमाः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चिन्तितः पुनरायाति चतुर्थे चेत्तदागमः॥४४८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If the Moon is in Sagittarius, Taurus, Aries or Leo, the man of whom one is thinking will return soon. If the Moon is in the 4th place, the man thought about will return. 448  

**स्वस्वर्क्षेषु च तिष्ठन्ति शुक्रजीवेन्दुसोमजाः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**प्रयाणागमने ब्रूयात्तत्तदाशासु सर्वदा॥४४९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If Venus, Jupiter, the Moon and Mercury are in their own houses, travel will take place in the direction in which the planets are situated. 449

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**ग्रहः स्वक्षेत्रमायाति यावत्तत्र फलं वदेत्।  
शुभग्रहवशात्सौख्यं पीडां पपग्रहैर्वदेत्॥४५०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 When the planets reach their own houses the fruits (benefits) of travel are to be told. Good and bad effects oftravel are to be predicted in terms of the strength or weakness of the planets. 450

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सप्तमाष्टमयोः पापास्तिष्ठन्ति च यदिग्रहाः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**प्रेषितो हृतसर्वस्वस्तत्रैव सरणं व्रजेत्॥४५१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If malefics are in the 7th and 8th places, the man who has gone on travel will be robbed of his property and killed too there. 451

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">
