**षष्ठे पापयुते मार्गे गामिबंधो भविष्यति।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जलराशौ स्थिते पापे चिरेणायाति जिन्तितः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**बलाबलानुरूपेण शुभाशुभनिरूपणम्॥४५२॥**  

 If a malefic is in the 6th place the man who has gone out will be imprisoned. If the malefic is in a watery sign, the man on travel will come back home after a long time. Good and bad effects of travel are to be predicted in terms of the strength or wekness of the planets. 452

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681980111.png)

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

**Chapter XXVI**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***OF RAINS***

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जलराशौ तु लग्ने वा जलग्रहनिरीक्षिते।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कथयेदृष्टिरस्तीति विपरीते न वर्षति॥४५३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Lagna is a watery sign or if it is aspected by a watery planet, the downpour of rain can be predicted. If it is otherwise, there will be no rainfall. 453

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जलराशिषु शुक्रेन्दु तिष्ठतो वृष्टिरुत्तमा।  
एतौ स्वक्षेत्रमुच्चं वा पश्यतो यदि केन्द्रगौ॥४५४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**त्रिचतुर्दिवसानन्तर्महावृष्टिर्भविष्यति।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**लग्नाच्चतुर्थे शुक्रस्स्यात्तद्दिने वृष्टिरुत्तमा॥४५५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Venus or the Moon is in a watery sign, there will be he heavy downpour; and if Venus or the Moon is aspecting their own housecs, or their exalted signs, or posited in their Kendras. heavy downpour within three or four days can be predicted. If Venus is in the 4th place, rain will fall on the same day when the Prasna is made. 454–455

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**जलराशिषु तिष्ठन्ति शुक्रजीवसुधाकराः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**आरूढोदयराशींश्चेत्पश्यन्त्यधिकवृष्टयः॥४५६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Venus, Jupiter, and the Moon are in watery signs, or aspect the Aaroodha or Udaya Raasi, there will be very heavy downpour. 456

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**छत्रे पृष्ठोदये जाते पृष्ठोदयग्रहेक्षिते।  
तत्काले परिवेषादौ दृष्टे वृष्टिर्महत्तरा॥४५७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Chhatra Raasi is a Prishthodaya sign and is aspected by a Prishthodaya planet and at the same time the Parivesha is also seen, heavy rainfall is most likely. 457

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**केन्द्रेषु मन्दभौमज्ञराहवो यदि संस्थिताः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**वृष्टिर्नास्तीति कथयेदथवा चण्डमारुतः॥४५८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Saturn, Mars, Mercury and Rahu are in Kendra, there will be no rainfall, but a big windstorm will blow. 458

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पापास्सौम्यविमिश्राश्चेदल्पवृष्टिर्भविष्यति।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चापस्थौ मन्दराहू चेद्वृष्टिर्नास्तीति कीर्तयेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुभः कार्मुकसंस्थश्चद्धोरा वृष्टिर्भविष्यति॥४५९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If malefics are associated with benefics in a Kendra, the rainfall will be little. If Rahu and Saturn are in Sagittarius at the time of Prasna there will be no rainfall. But if benefics are in Sagittarius, there will be heavy rainfall. 459

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**उच्चेन युक्ते दृष्टे वा त्वर्घवृद्धिर्भविष्यति।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**नीचेन युक्ते दृष्टे वा स्यादर्घक्षय ईरितः॥४६०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Udaya Lagna is associated with or aspected by a planet in exaltation there will be an increase in prices of commodities. There will be fall in prices, if it is aspected by or associated with debilitated planets. 460

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**मित्रस्वामिवशात्साम्यमेवं ज्ञात्वा वदेत्सुधीः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**शुभग्रहयुते वृद्धिरशुभेर्घस्य नाशनम्॥४६१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The prices will be moderate, if the Lagna is aspected by or assocfated with a friendly planet or the lord of the Lagna. If a benefic is associated with the Lagnaj. the prices will increase; and if a malefic, the prices will fall. 461

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681980428.png)  
**Chapter**XXVII**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***OF SHIPS***

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**जलराशिषु लग्नेषु जीवशुक्रेन्दवो यदि।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पोतसस्यशागमनं ब्रूयादशुभाश्चे न्नहीति च॥४६२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If Prasna is made about the arrival of ships, the method of answering is given below:–  
 If the Lagna is a watery sign, and if Jupiter, Venus, or the Moon is posited there, the arrival of ships is to be stated. But if malefics are in the Lagna, no ship will come. 462  

**आरूढच्छत्रलग्नेषु वीक्षितेष्वशुभग्रहैः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पोतभंगो भवेन्नीचशत्रुभिर्वा तथा वदेत्॥४६३॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If malefics aspect the Aaroodha or Chhatra Lagna, the ship will sink. Even if debilitated planets or inimical planets aspect the above Lagnas, damage to the ship is to be predicted. 463

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**अपृष्ठभोदये लग्ने दृष्टे देशात्तु नौर्व्रजेत्।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**तद्ग्रहेतु यदा दृष्टे तदा नौदर्शनं भवेत्॥४६४॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 If the Lagna is other than a Prishthodaya Raasi, and if the Udaya Lagna is aspected by its lord, the ship will leave thecountry of destination. When the lord of the Lagna is aspected by another planet, the ship will be sighted. 464

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**चरराशौ चरच्छत्रे द्रुतमायाति नौस्तदा।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चतुर्थे पञ्चमे चन्द्रो यदि नौः शीघ्रमेष्यति॥४६५॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If either the Prasna Lagna or the Chhatra Raasi is a moveable sign, the ship will arrive soon. If the Moon is in the 4th or 5th place, the ship will come very soon. If Venus is in the 2nd or 3rd place, the ship will arrive. Like–wise should other predictions be made after careful investigation. 465

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

![](../books_images/1681980773.png)  
**Chapter XXVIII**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


***ACHIEVEMENT***

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**द्वितीये वा तृतीये वा शुक्रश्चेन्नौसमागमः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**अनेनैव क्रमैणैवं सर्वं वीक्ष्य वदेत्स्फुटम्॥४६६॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**लग्नस्थौ कार्यलग्नेशौ कार्यस्थौ लग्नकार्यपौ।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कार्यस्य सिद्धिं कुरुतस्तदानीं निश्चयाद्वदेत्॥४६७॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**लग्नं लग्नेश्वरः पश्येत्कार्यं पश्येत्तु कार्यपः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कार्येश्वरो लग्नगतः प्रपश्ये ल्लग्नपं तथा॥४६८॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


**वा विलग्नपतिः कार्यगृहस्थः कार्यपं तथा।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**पश्येल्लग्नाधिपः कार्यं लग्नं कार्यपतिस्तथा॥४६९॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**कार्येशोलग्नपं पश्येल्लग्नेशः कार्यपं तथा।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**चन्द्रदृष्टिर्यदा चेत्स्यात्कार्यसिद्धिस्तदा स्मृता॥४७०॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 The time when the work will be accomplished is stated here: There are seven Yogas when a work will be accomplished successfully: (1) When the lord of the Lagna and the lord of the 10th house are in the 10th place; (2) when the lord of the 10th house and the lord of the Lagna are in Lagna; (3) when the Lagna is aspected by the lord of the Lagna or when the lord of the 10th house aspects the 10thhouse; (4) when the lord of the 10th house is in Lagna and aspects the lord of the Lagna; (5) when the lord of the. Lagna is in the 10th house and aspects the lord of the 10th house; (6) when the lord of the Lagna aspects the 10th house and the lord of the 10th aspects the Lagna; and (7) when the lord of the 10th aspects the lord of the Lagna and the lord of the Lagna aspects the lord of the 10th. When the Moon aspects any of the above Yogas, certain accomplishment of the deed is predicted. 466–470  

**असत्स्वपि च योगेघु कार्येशो लग्नराशिगः।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**भविष्यति तदा काले कार्यं ज्ञानप्रदीपके॥४७१॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">


 Even if these Yogas are not available, when the lord of the 10th house during his usual transit reaches the Lagna, the achievement of the work is to be predicted, says the science of *Gnaanapradeepikaa*. 471

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**सम्यग्विचार्य प्रवदेन्न मिथ्यावाग्भविष्यति।**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

**प्रश्नादर्शमिदं शास्त्रं पृथिच्यांलोकभूषणम्॥४७२॥**

</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">



</div>

<div style="text-align:justify">

 If one carefully studies this science and gives his prediction after proper investigation, his words will not become a lie. This science of Prasna is an ornament to the world, provided it is applied rightly.472

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">


**PRASNA AAROODHA* *

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">

**OR PROBLEM SOLVING  
ASTROLOGY ENDS**

</div>

<div style="text-align:center">



</div>

।   **GLOSSARY**   ।                                                                 ।
।       Amsa       ।                        ... Part, Portion                        ।
।     Apachaya     ।                   ... 1,2,4,7 and 8th houses                    ।
।    Aapoklima     ।                    ... 3,6,9 and 12th houses                    ।
।     Aarohana     ।                    ... Ascendiring direction                    ।
।     Aaroodha     ।                 ... Direction where one stands                  ।
।      Asubha      ।                        ... inauspicious                         ।
।    Avarohana     ।                    ... Descending direction                     ।
।      Bhaava      ।                            ... House                            ।
।      Budha       ।                           ... Mercury                           ।
।     Chandra      ।                          ... The Moon                           ।
।   Chara Raasi    ।                        ... Moveable sign                        ।
।      Dasaa       ।                      ... Planetary period                       ।
।      Dhanus      ।                         ... Sagittarius                         ।
।       Dik        ।                          ... Direction                          ।
।    Drekkaana     ।                ... One–third division of a sign                 ।
।     Dakshina     ।                            ... South                            ।
।      Ghati       ।              ... A time period equal to 24 minutes              ।
।       Guru       ।                           ... Jupiter                           ।
।      Horaa       ।                  ... Half a division of a sign                  ।
।      Kanyaa      ।                            ... Virgo                            ।
।      Karma       । ... Literally, action; philosophically moral law of consequence ।
।      Kataka      ।                           ... Cancer                            ।
।      Kendra      ।                          ... Quadrant                           ।
।       Ketu       ।                ... Planet signifying Moon's Node                ।
।   Kroora Raasi   ।                         ... Cruel sign                          ।
।       Kuja       ।                            ... Mars                             ।
।      Kumbha      ।                          ... Aquarius                           ।
।      Makara      ।                          ... Capricorn                          ।
।     Maaraka      ।                   ... Death–inflicting planet                   ।
।      Mesha       ।                            ... Aries                            ।
।      Mithna      ।                           ... Gemini                            ।
।     Muhurta      ।          ... Auspicious time; duration of 1 1/2 hours           ।
।    Nakshatra     ।                            ... Star                             ।
।     Navaamsa     ।                ... One–ninth divission of a sign                ।
।      Neecha      ।                        ... Debilitation                         ।
।      Paapa       ।                       ... Malefic Planet                        ।
।    Panaphara     ।                    ... 2,5,8 and 11th houses                    ।
।     Paschima     ।                            ... West                             ।
।     Poorvee      ।                            ... East                             ।
।      Praaga      ।                            ... East                             ।
।      Prasna      ।                      ... Question, inquiry                      ।
।   Prasna Lagna   ।              ... Rising sign at the time of query               ।
।   Prushtodaya    ।                    ... Rising by hinder part                    ।
।       Rahu       ।               ... Planet representing Moon's node               ।
।      Raasi       ।                        ... Zodiacal sign                        ।
।       Sani       ।                           ... Saturn                            ।
।    Shadvarga     ।               ... Six kinds of division of a sign               ।
।      Subha       ।                     ... Auspicious, benefic                     ।
।     Sirodaya     ।                   ... Rising by the head–sign                   ।
।   Stree Raasi    ।                        ... Feminine sign                        ।
।   Sthira Rassi   ।                         ... Fixed sign                          ।
।      Sukra       ।                            ... Venus                            ।
।     Trikona      ।                            ... Trine                            ।
।      Tulaa       ।                            ... Libra                            ।
।   Udaya Lagna    ।                   ... Rising sign – Ascendant                   ।
। Ubhayodaya Raasi ।         ... Signs rising both by hinder and head sides          ।
।      Uccha       ।                         ... Exaltation                          ।
।     Upachaya     ।                   ... 3,6,10 and 11th houses                    ।
।      Vakra       ।                        ... retrogression                        ।
।     Vighati      ।       ... 1/60th part of a ghati or 1/60th of 24 minutes        ।
।    Vrishabha     ।                           ... Taurus                           ।
